Hu Hanmin's Critique of Current Malpractices 72

Construction Should Not Focus on Embellishment

Hu Hanmin, President of the Legislative Yuan, gave a speech entitled "Construction Should Not Focus on Embellishment" at the memorial week of the Yuan on the 24th of this month. His words hit the nail on the head regarding current malpractices. Excerpts are as follows:

(Beginning omitted) Recently, we have been promoting a thrift campaign, which includes financial resources, time, and talent. In addition to personal thrift, government agencies and organizations should also be thrifty. Government agencies, in terms of hiring and working hours, must examine whether they are appropriate and whether there is waste. The organizational laws of each agency often state, "The number of staff or secretaries in a certain section or department shall be between X and Y people." This gives us room for thrift. No agency should casually fill up the maximum number of personnel. Currently, many agencies hire people indiscriminately to accommodate those seeking positions, filling vacancies as if filling them would make the entire agency's work more intense. In reality, there is an unknown amount of waste. As for inappropriate hiring, employing people in fields they did not study, or studying fields they do not use, the losses for both the public and private sectors are even greater, and it is even further from the principle of thrift. That is even more unacceptable. The most important point in saving financial resources within government agencies is not to worry about appearances or focus on embellishment. Every penny must be used practically. It does not matter if the appearance is a little lacking. For example, the recent reception for the Danish Crown Prince seemed too focused on appearances, which goes against the principle of thrift. Furthermore, the self-sufficiency of officials should be frugal, and everyone should cultivate a habit of hard work and endurance. This is also very important. The Turkish Revolution was successful seven years ago, but their capital, Ankara, is still not very elaborate. According to what I saw a few years ago, the population there is only over 70,000, and only one new street has been built. Government offices are mostly simple and crude, but the revolutionary spirit of the staff is very strong. The old capital, Constantinople, has a population of 700,000 to 800,000, almost ten times that of Ankara, and all the buildings are very grand. The distance between the two places is just like that between our Nanjing and Shanghai, which can be reached in a few hours by train. However, the people in their government do not covet the comfort of Constantinople. The high officials in the government do not regard the old capital as a place to rest. They often go there, and everyone works diligently on government affairs in Ankara year-round, constantly striving for self-improvement, seeking to alleviate the suffering of the people, saving financial resources in everything, and striving to create wealth for the people. What should the so-called revolutionary bureaucrats in our government, who live a life of ease and luxury above all the people, think about this? Those who only know their own enjoyment and do not know the suffering of the people, are they revolutionary officials? They are clearly corrupt bureaucrats. If officials are lax and indifferent, how can the people be invigorated? Up and down are exhausted.

It is a sign of national demise. How can it be something that a revolutionary government of a newly emerging country should have?

Speaking of embellishment, it is not only intolerable to the thrift campaign but is also a major obstacle in our construction. In all our work, we must break the embellishment mentality. Once the embellishment mentality takes hold, everything will be superficial and deceptive, deceiving ourselves and others. Even if something is built, it will definitely be unusable, and it will not even be possible to rebuild it well in the future. We must also understand that revolution and embellishment are incompatible. Embellishment has the function of concealing mistakes. Concealing mistakes means not being willing to correct them, which means not being revolutionary. If we make mistakes in our work, we should not avoid them or gloss them over. We should admit and correct them. Only then will everything achieve true beauty and goodness. Currently, the actual political work is too poor. If we still have to be busy putting on a show and seeking false praise, we will become complacent and ignore our actual shortcomings even more. That would be even worse. For example, the recent reception for the Danish Crown Prince should have been limited to the normal etiquette of international relations. He was just passing through our country on a tour. Some people say that the municipal government demolished hundreds of thatched houses and small rooms for this reason. I have asked the municipal government authorities, and they said that this did not happen. I also hope that it is so. If there were any mistakes, the people should be compensated for such losses. As far as the capital is concerned, we hope to have good buildings, houses, and roads for the people to enjoy, but this requires our usual efforts and practical implementation. There is no need for temporary embellishment or a deceptive mindset. It is not shameful to have thatched houses alongside the roads, and there is no need to conceal them in front of a few foreign guests, causing many residents to be displaced. We should strive to ensure that people do not live in thatched houses, or, if people already live in thatched houses, build tiled houses beforehand and have the residents move from the thatched houses to the tiled houses before the Danish Crown Prince arrives. That would still be comforting. But if we only seek a slightly better superficial appearance and the internal suffering is thereby worsened, what is the point? Our municipal administration and all our political work really do not need to be like this. There are people living in thatched houses, or even without thatched houses to live in, not only in Nanjing but everywhere in the country. When we see such suffering among the people, we should step up our efforts to realize the construction revolution. If we do not do practical work but only focus on embellishment, what is the point of revolution? I am afraid that the embellishment skills of the former autocratic government were even better than ours. What do the people want us for? In the matter of receiving the Danish Crown Prince, we should also recognize and pay attention to other aspects from the perspective of our revolutionaries. In international etiquette, we only need to be appropriate, and those we welcome and admire are not necessarily ordinary people with status and qualifications. If a great revolutionary, a great scholar, or a great inventor who has made practical and significant contributions to society and humanity comes to our country, our government may as well treat him with even more enthusiasm and diligence than any emperor or president. However, everything should focus on a sincere expression of spirit, and there is no need for "hanging brocade on the forest" or "fattening guests," all kinds of embellishment and false formality. This point is something our comrades must know.

If we extend the embellishment mentality to society for observation, it becomes even more frightening. Recently, a female comrade came to see me and talked about the situation in society. She said, "The income of people serving society has increased compared to the past, but everyone's life is more difficult and there are more problems because household expenses are many times higher than in the past. Of course, the prices of necessities such as clothing, food, and housing are higher than in the past, so expenses are higher, but the consumption on entertainment and social activities is many times higher than in the past, almost occupying the same or even higher position as necessary living expenses. This is most unbearable." So-called entertainment and social activities are mostly superficial and embellishment of life. They are very elastic and should not be a burden. I have repeatedly said, why did Rome perish in the past? Why has Germany revived recently? Is it not because one was too fond of embellishment and went down the road of extravagance and debauchery, while the other sought practicality in everything and was constantly struggling hard? We are now building a nation and reviving it. The situation in Rome is something we should resolutely guard against, and the situation in Germany is something we should resolutely learn from. Judging from the actual situation, the difficulties we face in building our nation may not be less than those faced by Germany, but the social atmosphere of valuing superficiality and not valuing practicality has always been the opposite of Germany's. Is that not dangerous?

Speaking of the social embellishment disease, it is necessary to mention the women's issue. That female comrade also told me that the new-style women's stockings displayed in shops in Shanghai and Nanjing are as expensive as twenty-five yuan a pair. Other things can be imagined. This kind of thing is really too incompatible with our national conditions. Although only a very small number of people use these luxury goods, it is not a blessing for society. Women's wills are relatively weak, and they are especially easily tempted by things. Women do not have sufficient opportunities for education, but they have ample opportunities for temptation. Its influence is enough to shake the spirit of hard work and struggle in the whole society. Especially when women themselves are seeking liberation, how can they be liberated in this situation? The so-called women's rights will definitely not be won in this way. Even if they are won, they will only be lost at any time and cannot be maintained. If women do not build a good foundation for being human through learning, ability, and career, they will inevitably focus on superficial embellishment, even taking decoration as their only life, then they can only be men's toys and slaves to things. Old-fashioned women worked hard at home and still had considerable abilities. New-style women leave the family and go to society, seemingly liberated, but they do not have the true ability to serve society. As a result, they mostly become decorations in society, not only moving further away from the goal of liberation but even unknowingly ultimately becoming men's toys without realizing it. In Guangdong, the principal of a certain women's normal school was willing to marry a wealthy merchant in Southeast Asia as his seventh concubine. Everyone who heard about it was shocked. It turned out that although she was the principal of a normal school, she really did not have much knowledge and had been shocked by the temptation of material things all her life, unable to resist it. Therefore, she finally found herself in a position that old-fashioned women were unwilling to be in, and she felt that it was her destination. Is it not pitiful and lamentable?

Open Letter to Generals and Soldiers from the Central Propaganda Department 73

The Central Propaganda Department recently issued an open letter to revolutionary generals and soldiers. The original text is as follows:

For more than a decade since the founding of the Republic of China, disasters have followed one after another, and the people's livelihood has withered. Our party's Leader, Sun Yat-sen, keenly aware of the difficulties, led the revolution, managing painstakingly and struggling actively. It took forty years to achieve what we have today. In the process of revolution, relying on the strong and resolute will and the loyal and courageous spirit of struggle of our revolutionary generals and soldiers, adhering to the Leader's teachings, sharing common beliefs and守護, uniting as one, we finally swept away the stubborn and massive brutal warlords, allowing the unification of our Republic of China to be achieved and the peaceful construction of the Three Principles of the People to begin. This glorious achievement has long been recognized by the world, and it is what our revolutionary generals and soldiers should encourage each other with and maintain forever.

Now that unification has been achieved and tutelage government has begun, remnants of warlords such as Feng Yuxiang and others have repeatedly colluded with corrupt forces. There are even those who abandon themselves and betray their past revolutionary history and personality, echoing the corrupt forces, seeking opportunities to create chaos in order to subvert the Party and the country that our revolutionary generals and soldiers have painstakingly fought for. This has led to recurring rebellions and no peaceful days, and the construction work of our Party has also been greatly hindered. Thinking of this, we are truly heartbroken. Our revolutionary generals and soldiers should know that today's Party and country were created by the blood and sweat of our revolutionary generals and soldiers, and no reactionary remnant warlords are allowed to rise up and destroy them. Today, all the political programs and policies of the Central Government are implemented based on the Leader's teachings and the wishes of the people of the whole country, and no counter-revolutionary forces are allowed to rise up and resist them. In this regard, our revolutionary generals and soldiers should always maintain their patriotic and world-saving zeal, follow the Leader's teachings, distinguish right from wrong, understand the benefits and harms, support the Party and the country, and consolidate the Central Government. Then the achievements and honors of our revolutionary generals and soldiers will surely become greater and greater. The facts of the demise of reactionary remnant warlords in recent years prove that all those who support the Central Government and obey the Party's discipline prosper, while those who resist the Central Government and go against the will of the people perish. The trend of obedience and disobedience is the key to the success or failure of today's soldiers. This is a point that our revolutionary generals and soldiers should deeply understand and encourage each other with.

Furthermore, today's peaceful unification is the common aspiration of the whole country. However, peace does not mean seeking temporary stability, and unification does not mean seeking formality. Only true unification can achieve practical peace, and only thorough peace can achieve the practical effect of unification. Our Party establishes the country based on the Three Principles of the People. Only those who inherit the Leader's teachings and obey the Party's mission are qualified to speak of peace. The Central Government is the Central Government of the people of the whole country. Only those who obey the Central Government's orders and jointly plan the construction of the country are qualified to speak of unification. Those who go against this, such as those who regard the army as their personal force, are not allowed by the Party's unification policy. Those who are treacherous, fickle, collude with reactionaries, and repeatedly plot rebellions are even less forgivable by the people of the whole country who long for peace. Therefore, all those who compete with each other in cunning and scheming, are fickle, resist the Central Government, and attempt to carve out territory, no matter what name they borrow, are traitors to the Party and public enemies of the people. (To be continued)

Zhang Guangwu Who Assassinated Wu Luzhen (Continued) 74

Sentenced to Ten Years Imprisonment by the Shandong High Court

(2) Submitting two types of evidence, 'The Qing History Romance' and 'Unofficial History of the Qing Dynasty', briefly stating that the name and occupation of the assassin of Wu Luzhen were detailed in the above two books and had no relationship whatsoever with Guangwu. How could there be arbitrary slander, and so on. Upon examining the award certificates, it could only be proven that before the Xinhai year, the defendant had served as the battalion commander of the First Garrison Regiment, and after the Xinhai year, the defendant had served as an army officer in the First Division Headquarters. As for what position he held in the Xinhai year (the year the martyr was assassinated), there was no document to prove it. Although it was said that he had requested leave to return home due to paralysis, since there was no order approved by his superior officer, nor any official document of handover, it was not credible. If it was said that this was the practice, then why was there a stamped approval later for leave due to injury (injury sustained in Mongolia, attached to the file of the Taian County Court, reviewed by the Chahar Commander). Moreover, the month and day of requesting leave in the Xinhai year was initially said to be in October (see the county file), then said to be in August (see the transcript of this court), intending to evade the period when the martyr was assassinated (November of the Xinhai year). The statements were contradictory and the defendant could not explain himself. Furthermore, the defendant's troops initially belonged to Tie Liang and ended with Yin Chang (see the defendant's statement), and finally belonged to Yuan Shikai (see the Qing History Romance). The claim that Yuan and Yin were the instigators of the assassination of Wu had no impact on the defendant's suspicion of committing a crime. Moreover, it has long been the public opinion that the assassination of the martyr was instigated by people like Tie Liang and Yin Chang. Even if the defendant did not serve as a battalion commander under Yuan Shikai, it cannot be used as an argument that he did not assassinate Wu. His first counter-evidence was not sufficient. Further review of 'The Qing History Romance' and 'Unofficial History of the Qing Dynasty' showed that they were both private writings. Although they were said to contain accurate records, they only revealed the main points. Furthermore, according to their contents, they were cross-referenced. 'The Qing History Romance' stated that the martyr was assassinated by his subordinates Zhou Fulin and Wu Hongchang, etc. 'The Unofficial History of the Qing Dynasty' stated that the martyr was at the station with a certain Zhan drafting a telegram when a soldier Ma Zhongtian entered, congratulating Fu Jinxi. He then drew a knife from his boot and slashed directly. The martyr resisted from his seat and Zhan also shouted. Upon hearing this, the accomplice soldiers immediately entered and attacked in a crowd, cutting off the martyr's head to bring to Beijing, etc. It was clear that not only those who participated in the conspiracy to assassinate the martyr were numerous, but also those who carried out the assassination were in the majority. As for the names of all the people involved, apart from the ringleader, even if the author had investigated each one, there was no need to disclose them all in the novel. How could the defendant use the fact that only Zhou Fulin, Ma Huitian, and Wu Hongchang were listed, without mentioning his name, as an excuse to try to cunningly evade responsibility. His second counter-evidence was also difficult to establish. (3) The application of the law. The defendant, having been bribed, joined the assassination group and harmed revolutionary pioneers. His aim was to counter the revolution and organize groups or meetings and perform important tasks, which constituted the crime of the former paragraph of Article 7 of the Anti-Revolutionary Punishment Law. Although this law had not been promulgated when the defendant committed the crime, Article 13, Section 2 of this law clearly stipulates that if the crime was committed before the promulgation of this law and had not been definitively judged, it should also be punished in accordance with this law, and should naturally apply retroactively. The defendant also jointly conspired to commit murder, which violated Article 284, Section 1, Item 1 of the Criminal Law. Since the crime was committed before the implementation of the Criminal Law, according to the provisions of the proviso of Article 2 of the Criminal Law, Article 311 of the Criminal Law, which stipulates a lighter punishment for the crime committed, should still be applied. According to Article 74 of the Criminal Law, one act constituting two crimes should be punished severely. Furthermore, the defendant was merely a military officer who only knew how to obey his superior officers, which led him to be caught in the legal net. Moreover, when the assassination was actually carried out, there were other ringleaders (Zhou Fulin, Ma Huitian). The defendant was an accessory, and it was not appropriate to impose a high sentence. Based on the above conclusions, the defendant Zhang Guangwu organized a group and performed important tasks with the aim of counter-revolution, and jointly conspired to commit murder. In accordance with the former paragraph of Article 7 and Section 2 of Article 13 of the Provisional Regulations on the Punishment of Counter-Revolutionaries, Article 311 of the Criminal Law, the proviso of Article 2 of the Criminal Law, Article 284, Section 1, Item 1, Article 74, Article 292, Article 56, Sections 2 and 3 of Article 57, Article 64, and Section 2 of Article 6 of the Implementing Regulations of the Criminal Law, he was sentenced to ten years of imprisonment and deprived of public rights for fifteen years within the scope of the original sentence. The number of days of detention before the judgment was determined was counted as one day of imprisonment for every two days. The judgment was specially made as in the main text.

This case was attended by Prosecutor Li Shicheng, who performed his duties. March 13, 1920 (19th year of the Republic of China), Judges Ouyang Xu, Liu Dexun, and Wang Mianshan, Clerk Zhao Zhu."

National Defense: After Liang's Death, Su Inherits the Border 76

Su Bingwen Inspects the Manchurian Border

White Russian Rebellion in Shiwei County

Harbin dispatch, 21st: After Liang Zhongjia's death, the Manchurian border becomes vitally important once again. In the Northeast, everyone recognizes its critical significance. When Wan Fulin was in Liaoning, he repeatedly consulted with Zhang Xueliang, Zhang Zuoxiang, Tang Yulin, and other key figures. The final decision was to have Su Bingwen succeed as commander of the 15th Brigade, concurrently serving as the Hulunbuir Garrison Commander and the Commander of the Harbin-Manchurian Border Railway Defense Army. Su previously served as the commander of the 6th Brigade of the Fengtian Army, the 12th Brigade, and the 17th Division. In 1918, he participated in the Allied Powers' expedition to Siberia. He is now being transferred from his position as the Director of the Heilongjiang Provincial Defense Preparatory Office and Chief of Staff of the Deputy Commander's Office in Jiangsheng. He is energetic and capable, and willing to take on responsibility. Entrusting him with this vital border defense position is considered appropriate. On the 13th of this month, Su arrived in Hulunbuir to take office. The Manchurian border was quite unsettled after Liang's death. Su specifically ordered the 43rd Regiment of his troops to return to Manchuria Station to assist in defense. Therefore, the garrison at Manchuria Station, in addition to the two regiments of the 2nd Cavalry Brigade, plus one regiment of the 15th Brigade, now numbers approximately 5,000 troops, which has stabilized public sentiment. On the 17th of this month, Su traveled from Hailar to inspect the Manchurian border, meeting with Chen Zhiyuan, the commander of the 2nd Cavalry Brigade, to discuss defense matters. On the 18th, he spoke with representatives from various local sectors, expressing his own views, stating that he had a deep personal friendship with Liang and would continue Liang's ambitions to strengthen the border defense. His key principles for action are: (1) Openness and honesty, and vigorously eliminating corruption; (2) Selecting talented individuals and rejecting villains; (3) Strictly enforcing discipline and setting an example with his own conduct; (4) Not fearing death and not loving money; (5) Being loyal to the Party and the nation. As for the remains of the soldiers who died in battle in the Zhalan Man area, many have already been recovered, and Su will be responsible for organizing a public burial at a fixed date. Memorial monuments will be erected next to the Zhalan Nuoer and Manchuria Station railways, and prominent figures of the Party and nation will be asked to write epitaphs on them. Construction has recently begun and is expected to be completed by mid-May. However, the harassment by Russian troops on the border has recently intensified. On the evening of the 17th of this month, 29 Russian cavalrymen penetrated our army's defense line in Zhalan Nuoer, still attempting to plunder guns and horses. They were detected by our army and driven out of the border, with one of them captured. He claimed that their entry was to search for Soviet people who were betraying their country, but his other words were evasive. The next day, he was claimed by the Russian consul. Again that evening, Russian troops conducted artillery exercises on the border for about 20 minutes before stopping. The merchants and residents in our territory are used to this and are not very alarmed. On the morning of the 18th, three Russian planes circled the Zhalan Man border for half an hour before landing at Dawuli. Other demonstrations, seemingly intentional or unintentional, are numerous. Fortunately, the authorities instructed their subordinates to maintain calm, so no incidents occurred.

Shiwei and Qigan counties are mostly inhabited by White Russian immigrants. Since the Russian unrest last year, the clever ones fled, while the poor ones were lured and threatened by the Red Russians, obeying their orders to engage in anti-Chinese actions. The White Russians in Shiwei, those in Xiaohezi, Wulongtao, Haidolai, Geshenge, and other places, have mutually connected to rebel, and have set up tax checkpoints at Wulongtao and Xiaohezi, collecting taxes and inspecting Chinese. Chinese people traveling between the two counties and inland are often killed and robbed. The Shiwei county government has been moved to Hewu because of this. Two thousand miles along the border have been occupied by Russia in an invisible way.

Hangzhou Quick Dispatch 77

The 29th is the 19th anniversary of the martyrdom of the 72 Martyrs of Huanghuagang. People from all walks of life have scheduled a mass rally at the public sports field at 1:00 PM to commemorate them. The preparatory committee has already notified various agencies and organizations to participate at that time.

The Zhejiang Provincial Industrial and Commercial Visiting Office has been established. Its operating expenses are estimated at over 4,900 yuan annually. It is planned to transfer the funds of the Zhejiang Branch of the National Goods Investigation Association for use. The Construction Department yesterday appointed Liu Yong and Wang Zhonglian as staff members of the office.

The Liangzhe Salt Affairs Audit Branch sent a telegram yesterday to the Wenchu General Tax Collector, stating that the post-war military expenses for the salt in Chu Prefecture have been approved to be reduced to 7.5 jiao per dan, and the military surtax has been reduced to 5 jiao per dan. All other salt fields are completely exempt. This will be implemented starting April 1st.

The price of rice in Hangzhou has been rising repeatedly. Top-quality rice is 16.2 yuan per shi, and ordinary rice is 13.4 yuan per shi. The source of rice is becoming less. Various rice shops have requested that the Rice Price Evaluation Council add 4 jiao to adjust the price. Yesterday, the council held a regular meeting. In order to take care of people's livelihood, it was decided to temporarily maintain the original price and then look at the market situation at the next regular meeting to discuss increasing or decreasing the price.

The seven porridge kitchens in Hangzhou City will be allowed to stop on the 31st. After the report is finished, the organization of the price-controlled rice sales will begin. There will also be seven locations and last for three months. The opening of rice sales is planned from May 1st to the end of July.

Songjiang 78

Minutes of the County Administration Meeting: The county government held its 51st county administration meeting on the 27th to discuss various cases. (1) It was discussed whether to approve the Construction Bureau's report on the reconstruction of Puzhao Temple Bridge. It was decided to approve it. (2) It was discussed how to deal with the issue of shop signs that cross the street both inside and outside the city and the two-step awnings of shops and households, which not only obstruct streetlights but are also related to fire prevention. It was decided that the county magistrate should instruct the Public Security Bureau's First District Office to persuade everyone to demolish them uniformly.

The Various Villages and Townships Under the County Repeatedly Report Robberies: After the neighboring Jinshan County was attacked and disturbed by bandits, robberies have been frequently reported in various places connected to this county. Bandits are as numerous as hair. Merchants and residents are panicked. At 1:00 AM on the night of the 27th, the home of Jiang Jing'an, a wealthy resident near Tangqiao in this county, was suddenly attacked by over ten bandits. Some held guns and other weapons, entered the house, and searched each room, losing no small amount of clothing and cash. Before leaving, they also shot and wounded the victim and left with loud cries. That same night, the home of Wang Shuqin in Dongwujiazhuang in Hengshan was also robbed by bandits. The bandits came by boat and all had firearms. Thirty dan of white rice were robbed, and one Yangcheng Lake boat moored at the river wharf was untied, loaded with rice, and escaped. Some say this gang may be from the troops of Taibao Ashu, so they paid attention to the boats and rice. It is said that it has not yet been reported to the county. Also, on the evening of the 24th, the home of He Guiming in Yangjiadu, Punan Shanyang, was attacked by over twenty bandits, each holding long knives, iron rulers, box guns, and other weapons, and lighting huge candles. They broke into the house and robbed the house, tying up all ten members of the victim's family, both old and young. He Guiming, his wife, and his second son, Wenru, were all wounded. The eldest son, Shuntang, heard the bandits enter the house and immediately jumped onto the roof, snuck to the neighbor's house, and shouted for help, and the bandits took the loot and left. It is said that 53 silver dollars, three gold rings, and cotton clothing were robbed. Today, the case has been reported to the Songjiang County Government for investigation and arrest.

Minutes of the Standing Committee of the Party and Government Committee: The Songjiang County Party Affairs Consolidation Committee held its 5th meeting on the 27th and resolved: (1) The price of rice has risen repeatedly, and people's food is worrying. It is urgent to organize price controls to benefit people's livelihood. It was resolved to forward the letter to the County Government for handling. (2) This Committee plans to hold a registration test for Party Boy Scout service members on March 28th. Please send personnel to supervise the test. It was resolved to recommend Comrade Zhang Huanzhi to supervise. (3) Expand propaganda to denounce Feng's rebellion. It was resolved to hand it over to the Propaganda Department for maximum handling. (4) A letter from the Provincial Secretariat stated that the former County Executive Committee had abused living expenses and disregarded public funds, hoping to order the repayment of the arrears. It was resolved to urge the former standing committee member in charge to recover the arrears. (5) Burning paper money during Qingming is superstitious and should be prohibited by the County Government to eliminate bad habits. It was resolved to forward it to the County Government for handling.

Another Large Batch of Refugees Arrives in Weiting: A large group of refugees suddenly arrived in Weiting, which belongs to the county, from the Kunshan area. Investigation of Prisoners in Custody Throughout the Province: Jiangsu Higher Court President Lin recently stated that the number of prisoners in custody in new and old prisons and detention centers throughout the province is extremely crowded, exceeding the approved capacity by more than half. It is urgent to translate this into an actual number of investigations. He ordered the wardens of each prison and the guards of each detention center to separate the crimes of prisoners in custody who have and have not been convicted and submit a written report for review. Now the wardens of each county, etc., have all submitted a reply as ordered. The most recent number of convicted and unconvicted prisoners in the province's prisons is recorded as follows: 9 sentenced to death, 543 to life imprisonment, 364 to imprisonment for more than 15 years, 1,306 to imprisonment for more than 10 years, 529 to imprisonment for more than 7 years, 774 to imprisonment for more than 5 years, 864 to imprisonment for more than 3 years, 1,555 to imprisonment for more than 1 year, 1,257 to imprisonment for more than 6 months, 1,446 to imprisonment for more than 2 months, 183 to imprisonment for less than 2 months, 207 to detention, 627 to imprisonment in lieu of a fine, and 11 others. The total is 9,675. Among the prisoners in custody, opium offenders account for 28-29% of the total, robbery, and pirates account for slightly less than 20%, theft accounts for 10%, injury and murder account for 10%, and special law offenders account for 9%.

Qingpu 81

Change of Director of the Finance Bureau: Zhang Zanshou, the Director of the Finance Bureau of this county, has applied for resignation due to personal reasons. It has been approved by the provincial government, and Wang Huazhao, the Director of the Finance Bureau of Kunshan County, has been appointed to fill the vacancy. Large Number of Lake Bandits Discovered in Xin Town: A large number of lake bandits were discovered in Xin Town, which belongs to Qingpu. There are more than 200 large and small bandit boats. The 400 to 500 bandits wear plain clothes with red cloth tied around their arms. Machine guns and box cannons are fully equipped. There have been daily reports of looting ships and requisitioning military supplies in Dingjiashed, Fengjing, and other nearby places. The water police team in Liantang has gathered only 17 patrol boats. The police force is weak and the situation is extremely dangerous. There are rumors that bandits will come to Zhujiajiao Town in the Second District to rob. Magistrate Shen has reported the situation to the Provincial Civil Affairs Department and requested a prompt dispatch of troops to station and defend the area.

Zhu Futang's House Robbed: The home of Zhu Futang, a farmer in Yejiabang, Qingpu, was suddenly attacked by over twenty bandits speaking with a Jiangbei accent at around 9:00 PM the day before yesterday. They were armed with wooden sticks and hard-cased guns, broke down the door and entered, turned over boxes and cabinets, and searched arbitrarily. They also beat the victim Zhu Futang and caused a loss of approximately 200 yuan. The local defense corps rushed to the scene upon hearing the news, but the bandits had already fled far away.

Wuxi 82

Convening a Conference to Suppress Bandits in Taihu Lake: Hu Zuyu, the commander-in-chief for suppressing bandits in Taihu Lake, has decided to launch a large-scale bandit suppression campaign within days. In order to determine the policy for suppressing bandits, he specifically scheduled the Second Taihu Bandit Suppression Conference to be held at noon on the 31st at the Suzhou Headquarters, convening the county magistrates, public security bureau chiefs, and water police district chiefs of the counties bordering Taihu Lake in southern Jiangsu. The Wuxi County Government and the Water Police District Public Security Bureau have received telegrams and are preparing to attend the meeting at that time. Furthermore, according to intelligence reports received yesterday by Mao Mujun, the commander of the Second Water Police District, a large team of lake bandits plans to split from Zhou Tieqiao and Caoqiao to Yixing Liyang, cross Nandumeizhu, and flee to Anhui Province. He immediately sent a telegram ordering Huang Chengji, the captain of the 9th team stationed in Yixing, to dispatch a team to intercept them.

The Origin of the Robbery Rumor in the Urban Area: The home of Gu Yaodou on Xiaohe Shang in Wuxi City was suddenly attacked by six thugs at around 7:00 PM the day before yesterday. They went straight upstairs and searched repeatedly but only found some old clothes and dozens of copper coins. They roared loudly, and Gu's children were frightened and screamed for help. Neighbors gathered, and the thugs fired guns towards the Xinmiaoqian area and fled. For a time, it was rumored far and wide that a robbery had occurred in the urban area. Xu Yunsheng, a patrol leader from the First Branch of the Public Security Bureau, immediately led the police to investigate upon hearing the report. It was only then learned that Wang Guifang, a clerk from the Second Squad of the County Police Team, had led plainclothes detectives to Gu's house to investigate opium, but he had not explained the reason, which led to the suspicion of robbery.

County Magistrate Sun Applies for Resignation: Sun Zuji, the County Magistrate and Director of the Municipal Preparatory Office of this county, has served for one year since taking office. On the 24th of this month, he submitted a report to Ye Chucang, the Chairman of the Jiangsu Provincial Government, requesting resignation and asking for the appointment of another capable official to replace him in Wuxi.

Commercial Corps Gun Accidentally Injures Two People: Zhang F茂, a member of the 36th detachment of the Yangshuyuan Township Commercial Corps in Wan'an City, accidentally fired a handgun while wiping it in the team headquarters at 10:00 AM yesterday. The bullet struck the waist of Ge Wangqi, a corps member standing nearby watching, entering from the right waist, piercing the large intestine, and exiting from the back. It also injured Yu Boqian's right foot. Both immediately fell to the ground in extreme pain, with blood flowing like a stream. Later, both Ge and Yu were sent to Puren Hospital by boat by their companions for treatment. It is reported that Ge Wangqi's injuries are quite dangerous. If there are no changes within three days, his life may be saved. Yu Boqian only injured his skin and was discharged after being slightly bandaged.

The Municipal Preparatory Office Is Scheduled to Close: Director Sun, who is also the director of the Wuxi Municipal Preparatory Office, stated that the office has been ordered to stop operations and will close at the end of March. However, it was decided to hold the 34th office meeting yesterday to decide whether each department should appoint a custodian to be responsible for safekeeping. The decisions were: (1) To recommend Jiang Zumin, Chen Hongzao, and others as custodians. (2) The health instructor and street sweepers will continue to work as usual. (3) To submit a report to the provincial government requesting the prompt issuance of regulations for reorganizing the municipal committee to facilitate the transfer. (4) The closing meeting is scheduled to be held at 2:00 PM on the 31st of this month.

Changzhou 83

Another Thief Apprehended Near Qishuyan: The Commercial Corps Branch of Qishuyan Town in Wuyi County has cracked the robbery case near Hulutou, etc., in the town and arrested four thieves, including Gao Jincan, who have been transferred to the court for interrogation. The Commercial Corps Branch learned that the thief Sheng Peiji had confessed in the branch that an accomplice, Liu Bingwen, lived in Xin'an Town, etc., so it immediately sent a confidential letter to the Xin'an Commercial Corps Branch, asking them to arrest him nearby. They soon captured Liu and transferred him to Qishuyan on the 27th. The Qishuyan Town Commercial Corps Branch Chief then handed him over to the county for legal action.

The Slapping Case in the County Court: Ding Hong, a clerk in the trial division of the Wuyi County Court, had an argument with accountant Huang Xiaoshan when he borrowed his salary from the accounting office on the 27th. Wang Jinghu, a recorder in charge of the stolen goods warehouse, spoke up in his defense. A disagreement broke out, and Wang slapped Ding Hong in the face. Ding was unwilling to accept this and immediately filed a lawsuit with the prosecutor's office, which was sent to the trial division for public judgment. The case was heard by Tong Weishi, who summoned the defendants and witnesses for interrogation. As a result, Wang Jinghu was found guilty of injuring Ding Hong and sentenced to seven days of detention. He was also sentenced to seven days of detention for violating the Party's regulations on disciplinary punishment. Both sentences were combined, and Wang Jinghu was sentenced to 14 days of detention. Wang Jinghu requested bail in court. Judge Tong approved his bail and the execution of the sentence will be carried out after the appeal period.

Zhenjiang 84

The Railway Bureau Plans to Move the Zhenjiang Small Station: The Zhenjiang Small Station is located next to the Xiaomatou on the riverbank. Every time the water source dries up in winter, loading and unloading goods is quite inconvenient, affecting commerce and causing no small impact. The Zhenjiang Chamber of Commerce specifically telegraphed the Ministry of Railways, requesting the relocation of the small station to the Yangguan area to benefit commerce. The Ministry of Railways has approved the request and ordered the Beijing-Shanghai Railway Bureau to investigate and handle it. Yesterday, the bureau specifically sent Liu Weibin, the Director of the Railway Administration Department, to Zhenjiang to inspect the terrain. The plan is to move it to the vicinity of the China Merchants Wharf. Construction is expected to begin soon. Jiangsu Provincial National Exhibition to Open: The Jiangsu Provincial National Goods Exhibition held its third standing committee meeting at the Zhenjiang County Party Headquarters yesterday. It was decided that the opening date will be tentatively set for April 10th. Another meeting will be held on the 31st of this month to convene a representative assembly to discuss all the progress.

The Jiangsu Farmers Bank Plans to Move to Zhenjiang: The Jiangsu Provincial Farmers Bank was previously located in Nanjing because the provincial government was located there. Now that the provincial government has moved to Zhenjiang for over a year, the bank is also operated by the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Agriculture, so it is necessary to move to Zhenjiang for convenience. Therefore, it is also planning to move to Zhenjiang to operate. Yesterday, personnel were sent to Zhenjiang to prepare everything.

Yangzhou 85

Thieves Who Killed Three People Apprehended: Chu Faji and his granddaughter were robbed and hacked to death in the back of Tongjia Lane, Daqiao East Street, and Chu's wife Wu was injured in the same case. It is now learned that Wu has died from her injuries. On the morning of the 27th, Han Wenzhu, the captain of the police squadron, led detectives Shao Shigui and Chen Yongzhao to arrest the thieves Wu Hengxing and Meng Yicheng outside Xu Ningmen and arrested Li Er, Zhu Shunyin, and the owner of the Nanyang Hotel, Wang Guisheng, at the lacquerware alley Nanyang Hotel, for preliminary interrogation. It was learned that there were a total of ten accomplices in the case. Many are still at large and are being investigated.

Petition to Dredge the Silted Yi River: Zhang Jiarui, the Huaiyun Envoy, has now received a report from Li Neimin, the manager of the Yangzi Salt Depot, that the Yi River is silted up, which hinders salt transportation, and requesting construction to dredge the river. After receiving the report yesterday (26th), Zhang, in addition to submitting it to the Salt Affairs Administration for review due to a shortage of funds, specifically ordered the salt depot to comply with the instructions after the Salt Affairs Administration approves and instructs.

Provincial Order to Reconsider the Commutation of Labor Service: The county government submitted a report to the Construction Department for review regarding the resolution of the second county administration meeting to limit the commutation of labor service for road construction to five yuan across the board. An instruction has now been received to collect the total amount by calculating the amount of earthwork each person should build, according to the local price per cubic foot. Yesterday (26th), the Construction Bureau was specifically ordered to review the matter and submit it to the county for transfer.

The Date of Construction and Establishment of the County Court: The Jiangdu County Court has discussed the fundraising and reconstruction of the court site multiple times. Yesterday (27th), the fourth preparatory meeting was held to resolve that the reconstruction project will be contracted to Zhang Wantai Tile and Wood Factory, which offered the lowest price of 2,897 yuan. It is also heard that the repairs are scheduled to be completed in one month, and the court's establishment date is said to be around May 1st.

Taizhou 86

Communists Burn and Kill in Xiaoxi Village: In recent days, over a thousand communists have gathered in the western townships of Linhai, disarming, burning, and killing in Yancun. Colonel Zhu of the Fifth Regiment stationed in Jiao (Haimen) was ordered to lead a large force concentrated in this city to prepare for an attack. Unexpectedly, a part of the communists, about two hundred people, burned over a hundred houses of residents such as Qin Yan You in Shuixi Village in the southern township of this county at 2:00 PM yesterday (22nd) and shot and killed many people. Colonel Zhu heard the news and immediately sent Battalion Commander Xu Zhenhan of the Third Battalion to rush to the scene to suppress them. The communists retreated to the western townships.

Two Criminals Executed by Firing Squad: The Provincial Defense Army stationed in Linhai City arrested two criminals, Cheng Dailang and 麻面松, in the city the day before yesterday and sent them to the regiment headquarters. After the regiment commander interrogated them and confirmed the facts, they were bound and sent outside the West Gate yesterday (22nd) for execution by firing squad.

Huzhou 87

Robbery Occurs in Pantang: Zhang Yuanhua, a resident of Pantang, about five miles outside the South Gate of this city, was suddenly attacked by two bandit boats and over ten bandits armed with guns at around 2:00 AM on the 25th. They broke through the back door and entered, arbitrarily looting all the clothes, quilts, and over ten silver dollars. The village's volunteer defense corps heard about the incident, gathered the corps members, and rushed to the scene armed with guns, but the bandits had already escaped by boat to the north. Several bandits who were unable to get on the boat fled into the mountains. The corps members bravely pursued and captured two bandits who were unable to resist. They were escorted to the Second Regiment headquarters in this city by the corps at 2:00 PM yesterday for interrogation.

Wang Jinsheng Abducted in Zhaocun: Zhaocun, about three miles from Hejiabu in the western townships of Huzhou, was suddenly attacked by seven or eight bandits armed with handguns and flashlights at around 9:00 PM on the 24th. They broke into the home of Wang Jinsheng, the village chief, robbed him, and abducted Wang Jinsheng before leaving.

Xiaoshan 88

Budget for the First Section of the Xiao-Chang Road: The cost of the first section of the Xiaochang Light Railway, including culverts, machinery, and roadbed construction, is estimated to be 400,000 yuan: (1) Roadbed construction cost 208,344 yuan; (2) Bridge and culvert machinery cost 151,273.2 yuan; (3) Machine factory buildings cost 51,150 yuan. The bureau has submitted a request to the Construction Department to forward it to the Provincial Government to order the Finance Department to allocate the funds as soon as possible.

Investigation and Collection of Autonomous Donation: The Xiaoshan Autonomous Household Donation is to be completed uniformly by the county magistrate by April 30th of this year. The village committees have started the investigation on the 25th of this month. Ningbo 89

Chairman Jiang Inspects Xiangshan Port: Chairman Jiang ordered Navy Commander Chen Shaokuan to return to Shanghai with the Chu Tai warship yesterday to defend the secondary defense line and order them to report to Nanjing about the situation in Feng. Later, because Chairman Jiang suddenly wanted to inspect Xiangshan Port earlier, he ordered Commander Chen to slow down and telegraphed the Chu Tai warship, which was en route, to turn to Xiangshan Port to await orders. Chairman Jiang, together with Song Meiling, Song Zi'an, and his entourage adjutants, came to Yongbo by car from Xikou, Fenghua at 7:00 AM yesterday (February 26th). He then went to the Yongning Wharf on the north shore and was welcomed by Commander Chen onto the Jiankang warship. He immediately ordered the departure and sailed directly to Xiangshan Port, arriving at 11:30 AM. At that time, the Chu Tai warship had already arrived first. At around 2:00 PM, the inspection was completed, and the order was given to return. At 6:15 PM, it arrived in Yongbo and moored at the Yongning Wharf again. Commander Wang and Public Security Bureau Chief Mao, and others led the military and police to the wharf to welcome him. After Chairman Jiang, his wife, Commander Chen, Song Zi'an, and others disembarked, they returned to Xikou, Fenghua, by car. The Chu Tai warship was ordered to return to the Yong River to await orders and will arrive today. It is heard that Chairman Jiang will take the ship back to Nanjing after the ship arrives and will not transfer via Hangzhou.

Local News

Today, All Circles Commemorate the Yellow Flower Mound Martyrs 91

Meeting at the City Party Headquarters at 9:00 AM

Navy Gun Salute at Noon, Citywide Silence

Memorial Ceremonies Held Separately in Various Locations

Today is the 19th Anniversary of the Martyrdom of the Seventy-Two Martyrs of Yellow Flower Mound. The Publicity Department of the Municipal Executive Committee has repeatedly reported on the preparations for the memorial events of this day in this newspaper. It is now reported that all arrangements have been completed. At 9:00 AM today, a memorial meeting will be held in the auditorium on the third floor of the Municipal Party Headquarters. The department has notified various agencies, organizations, schools, and party branches at all levels to send four representatives each to participate in a unified expression of condolences. Zhenru, Meilong, Pudong, Jiangwan, and Wu districts will convene memorial meetings separately by their respective party branches, in accordance with the methods promulgated by the Municipal Publicity Department, gathering people from all walks of life in those areas. In addition to participating in the meeting convened by the Municipal Executive Committee, many agencies and organizations will also convene separate meetings of their own to commemorate the occasion. Furthermore, the methods of commemoration for today, in addition to holding memorial ceremonies, include (1) a day off, (2) flags at half-mast in the afternoon, (3) public officials and party members wearing black armbands for the day, (4) cessation of entertainment and banquets for the day, and (5) a five-minute silence at noon (signaled by a naval gun salute). These five items have been announced by the party and government authorities for public knowledge. The Municipal Executive Committee issued three types of announcements yesterday: "A Message to Comrades," "A Message to the People," and leaflets (lengthy excerpts omitted).

The Provisional Court and Court of Appeals of the Public Concession will, as usual, suspend hearings and judicial administration for one day today in commemoration of the Seventy-Two Martyrs of Yellow Flower Mound. This has been announced by President Xu for public awareness, and the police have been notified to suspend the transfer of cases. The flag will also be flown at half-mast today to express mourning.

Continuing the Revolutionary Spirit of the Seventy-Two Martyrs 92

(1) The commemoration of the martyrdom of the Seventy-Two Martyrs on March 29th is a memorial day for the comrades of our party who, in the year before the founding of the Republic of China, on March 29th, sought to establish Guangzhou as a revolutionary base with a spirit of benevolence and righteousness. The event was unsuccessful, and the seventy-two martyrs sacrificed themselves at Yellow Flower Mound. (2) The success of the Xinhai Revolution by our party, the establishment of a republican government, the stabilization of the foundation of the Republic of China, and the ability of our party to transition from military to tutelary government, to eliminate reactionaries, to unify the country, and to develop the spirit of party governance over the past nineteen years are all the result of the late Premier's painstaking efforts and the heroic and inspiring courage and spirit of the martyrs who died at Yellow Flower Mound. (3) In commemorating March 29th, we should follow the bloodstained footsteps of the martyrs, strive to overthrow imperialism, thoroughly eliminate the Communist Party, the National Socialist Party, the Reorganization Faction, and eradicate new and old warlords who collude with reactionaries, undermine unity, and bring disaster to the country and its people. (4) In commemorating March 29th, we must awaken the people, support the central government, consolidate unity, work hard on tutelary government construction, implement revolutionary diplomacy, and complete the cause of the rejuvenation of the Chinese nation, which is sufficient to honor the martyrs and fulfill the responsibilities of those who come after them.

The Rice Market Has Eased Slightly 95

The Social Bureau Secretly Investigates Rice Markets in the North and South

According to the Wuchen News Agency, rice prices have been rising continuously in recent days, reaching a maximum of over twenty yuan. The Social Bureau has already announced price limits and formulated emergency measures, and has submitted them to the mayor and ordered the rice industry groups to handle them. This was reported in yesterday's newspaper. It is now learned that yesterday there were 38 rice boats accumulated in the southern city, about 5,000+ shi, of which more than 3,000 shi had been sold by a certain major rice merchant. but none have been sold retail. This is truly unusual and a concern for the people's livelihood. The rice market in the city is still stagnant, and goods have yet to arrive. However, the price increases have eased compared to yesterday. It is reported that the Social Bureau yesterday sent personnel to secretly investigate the rice markets in the north and south at any time, so as to cooperate with the Public Security Bureau to implement crackdowns and maintain the people's food supply.

This City Will Organize a Rice Price Stabilization Committee 96

The Shanghai Municipal Food Committee, in view of the recent soaring rice prices and the people's food security being in danger, has drafted a plan to purchase 200,000 bags of foreign rice, with the months of May, June, July, August, and September as the period for handling the price-stabilized rice. If it is insufficient, additional purchases will be made at any time, and a Rice Price Stabilization Committee will be organized to handle all matters such as procurement, distribution, and other affairs, with dedicated responsibility. It has been submitted to the Social Bureau for submission to the Municipal Government, and approval has been granted to organize and establish it on an expedited basis. It is reported that, in addition to the members appointed by various bureaus of the Municipal Government, the remaining members will be nominated by local groups and invited to be appointed.

Chinese Face Obstacles Everywhere 97

Various Obstacles to Traveling Abroad

Chinese Citizens Going to Japan Are Again Being Sent Back. Since the beginning of this month on the 11th, Japan has rigorously enforced a ban on Chinese citizens with ancestry in Fujian and an absolute prohibition on Chinese laborers from going to Japan. The inspection of ships from Shanghai to Japan is extremely strict. There is almost no ship on which Chinese are not prevented from landing. In the month of March alone, more than one hundred Chinese citizens have been sent back to Shanghai. This time, a large number of Chinese citizens from Osaka, Nagoya, Yokohama, etc., were prohibited from landing by the Japanese Maritime Police and escorted back to Shanghai. These included He Peigen, Xu Kangpei, Pan Jichang, Jin Yaoming (Jin, a student, was also prohibited from entering the country), Li Liren, Li Liquan, Ren Huida (all Fujianese, are kimono merchants), Weng Jikang, Lin Guo, Liang, Lin Yule, Weng Guifa, Lin Guangzuo, Lin Xuehua, Lin Zhenxing, Xue Wensheng, Li Junguang, Lin Xiaofu, etc., totaling more than 20 people. Most of them wanted to land in Yokohama to go to the Akasaka district of Tokyo. Japan, citing violations of immigration regulations, rejected them all. Everyone traveled back and forth in vain and suffered huge losses.

Travel Passports Are Difficult to Obtain. In the past, Chinese citizens traveling to various countries only needed a business to act as a guarantor to obtain a passport. Recently, the Foreign Affairs Section of the Public Security Bureau has announced that Chinese citizens traveling to various countries to obtain passports to travel abroad have changed their new rules. Whether traveling to Europe, America, or Nanyang Singapore, etc., when applying for a passport, it must be guaranteed by a statutory authority to be valid. Otherwise, the consuls of the relevant countries will refuse to sign. Recently, due to passport crackdowns, many batches of people have been prevented from traveling abroad and unable to leave.

More Than Thirty Organizations Oppose Japan's Exclusion of Overseas Chinese 98

More than thirty organizations in Shanghai, including the Special Municipality Stallholders, Brokers, etc., jointly issued a declaration opposing Japan's exclusion of Overseas Chinese, stating that the Japanese imperialists have bullied our country and harmed our compatriots for years. The facts and their brutality are already known to everyone, and even more so than other imperialists. The year before last, when our revolution was winning victories and advancing straight into Youyan, they disregarded international law and sent troops to Shandong, blocking our righteous army, killing our officials, seizing our property, and infringing on our national rights. Their violence and evil reached their extreme. Our people have endured humiliation and still have lingering pain to this day. However, new sorrows frequently come before the old hatreds are eliminated. The Japanese imperialists have recently become more extreme and more violent. For our citizens going to their country, they first make it difficult for them, then expel them, and do not allow them to land at all. It is already obvious and undeniable that they are disrespecting our nation, bullying our nation, and oppressing our nation. If our Chinese nation continues to be bullied, slaughtered, disrespected, and oppressed, and cannot enjoy the happiness of freedom and equality with other nations, even if civil rights are developed and people's livelihoods are prosperous, it will still lead to national subjugation and racial extinction. This matter concerns the foundation of the country and should be taken seriously. The members of this association vow to oppose it to the death and hope that all compatriots across the country will rise up together and continue to carry out economic sanctions against Japan to urge them to realize the situation. This declaration is hereby made for your consideration.

Both the Tu Dong and the Di Bao Are Abolished Simultaneously 100

Announcement by the County Government

Effective April 1st

The Shanghai County Government issued an announcement yesterday stating that Peng Liren, the District Chief of the Second District, reported that since the appointment of the township chiefs and deputy commissioners, the original Tu Dong (Map Directors) had already become mere figureheads. However, without a clear order of cancellation, they still felt inconvenienced regarding the authority of the township chiefs. Now that there is a clear order to cancel the Di Bao (Local Security), the Tu Dong, who have a related relationship with the Di Bao, should be abolished in advance so that the township chiefs can unify their authority and all matters can be implemented without hindrance. A written request was duly submitted, requesting the County Government to review and issue an announcement to cancel the Tu Dong so that it could be posted for public knowledge, which would be a public convenience. After submitting it to the County Political Affairs Meeting for discussion, it was decided that the County Government would issue an announcement on April 1st to abolish it simultaneously with the Di Bao. It is hereby announced that all Tu and Di Bao in this county will be abolished on April 1st, which has been announced to the public. Now that the County Political Affairs Meeting has decided that the Tu Dong and Di Bao should be abolished simultaneously, it should be done immediately. In addition to ordering the district chiefs to inform them, a public notice is hereby issued so that all the people of the county may know that all Tu Dong in this county will be abolished simultaneously with the Di Bao from April 1st. The original duties of the Tu Dong will be handled by the township offices. This announcement is hereby made.

Three Finnish female missionaries, including Ka Jiangte, were kidnapped by bandits in Jiangxi Province without a trace. To this day, they have not been rescued. Situation After the Continued Slowdown by Pharmacy Workers 104

Because the pharmacies in the Public Concession and the French Concession refused to mediate and settle unemployed workers, the slowdown continued today. On the doors of the pharmacies were stuck the words "The capitalists do not obey the mediation, the workers continue to slow down," and the capitalists also printed the approval documents of the Central Executive Committee of the Kuomintang, resolutely refusing to settle the workers. The police authorities, fearing that incidents would arise, sent additional police to protect the major pharmacies.

The Shanghai Special Municipal Student Union, in view of the re-emergence of the dispute over the settlement of pharmaceutical workers and the capitalists' refusal to accept the mediation of the Social Bureau, issued a declaration advising the labor side to consistently conduct orderly movements and the capitalist side to make sincere concessions, and to wait quietly for the party and government authorities to find a solution. In addition, the Shanghai Zhabei Water and Electricity Workers Union, the Steamboat Timber Workers Union, the Chinese and Foreign Cloth Industry Workers Union, and 32 other unions also issued declarations yesterday to support the pharmaceutical workers.

Important News About the Yangtze River Shipping Industry 105

Continued Dispatch of Troops to Escort Ships. The upper reaches of the Yangtze River from Yichang to Hankou are currently in a period of high cargo volume. In the upper reaches of Shashi and the lower reaches of Yichang, because bandits are rising up, nine ships on the upper river have been attacked. The other day, the Jialing Maru of the Nissin Company and others were also attacked by bandits in the upper reaches. Yesterday, the various shipping companies in Shanghai received telegrams from Hankou stating that in addition to the United Kingdom, the United States, and Japan dispatching warships to escort ships between Yichang and Shashi, twenty naval escorts will be added to each foreign ship to protect them. If necessary, the transport of passengers and cargo may be suspended. However, the Jianghe, Xianghe, Qinghe, and Shashi ships of Jardine Matheson and Butterfield & Swire will continue to sail as usual.

Japanese Merchants Add New Ships. The Japanese Shangchuan East Company in the upper reaches of the river originally had one ship, the Changfeng Maru, operating. Recently, because the river water sometimes rises and falls, the company has specially built a new shallow-water ship in Shanghai called the Zhonggu Maru, with a load capacity of 220 tons, which can travel on the upper reaches of the Sichuan River. It is approved to be added to the Yichang route next month.

The Volume of Foreign Tobacco Shipments Increases Sharply. The Yangtze River ports have a very large outlet for cigarettes. Since the May 30th Movement, the outlet for foreign tobacco in the Yangtze River ports had fallen to about 200 boxes per day. Chinese cigarettes increased to about 1,600 or 1,700 boxes per day. By this year, since the Nanyang factory closed down, the export volume of Chinese cigarettes in the Yangtze River has plummeted. Recently, only 100 or 200 boxes are shipped. However, the export volume of cigarettes from British and American companies has increased sharply. At most, there are more than 3,000 boxes shipped to the Yangtze River ports every day. Recently, the average export volume is also about 1,600 or 1,700 boxes.

Great Competition in Sino-US Shipping Industry 106

Japanese Merchants Add Six Ships. This year, the Sino-US shipping industry competition... Japanese...with 85 million yuan...nine...join this...operate within, and the Osaka Company also invested an additional 30 million yuan and is building six new-style fast ships with strong rates in Japan. Each ship has a displacement of 13,000 tons and a net carrying capacity of 8,250 tons. All use motor engines, with a speed of 17 nautical miles per hour. Special silk cabins are built in each ship, which can hold 750 tons, and cold storage cabins can hold 350 tons. These six ships will operate exclusively between Shanghai and New York, taking the fastest sea route, limiting the journey from New York to Yokohama to only 28 days, and to Shanghai in just 35 days. Those who used to have a flight every three weeks now have a ship every fourteen days. Taking Shanghai as the main port in the Far East, it plans to take over the ports of Tianjin and Qingdao in North China to obtain the right to transport goods in North China. The first ship is scheduled to depart from Shanghai on July 7th, the second ship is scheduled to operate on July 19th, and by December 4th, all six new ships will be able to sail. It is expected that there will be the most intense competition on the Sino-US line this summer.

Raw Silk Freight Rates Fall Again. Pacific shipping companies have reduced Shanghai raw silk freight rates to US$1 per piece. Recently, the number of direct ships to New York has increased, and the raw silk freight rates have also been reduced. In order to compete for transportation, the Pacific shipping companies in Shanghai, and merchants in other places, have requested that the water rates for Chinese goods to the United States be reduced appropriately. After investigation by various railway companies, the shipping companies have received a reply that from May 1st, the train transfer fee for Shanghai raw silk transported to the United States and transferred to New York in San Francisco, Seattle, etc., will be reduced by one-third from US$9 per piece to US$6 per piece.

Advising Japanese Ships to Join the Association. British and American shipping merchants operating in the Pacific have recently held several meetings with the heads of various lines in the Far East. They all believe that the Japanese shipping companies that do not join the association arbitrarily reduce water rates, which makes the business suffer. After discussion, it was decided to advise Japanese merchants Kawasaki and Mitsui to also join the association. If they agree, the fee for transporting American silk can be increased by three yuan per piece, but the Japanese merchants have not yet accepted.

Records of Delayed Merchant Ships 107

Delayed by Fog. There was heavy fog in Shanghai again on the 27th. The foreign ships delayed by fog outside Wusong included the China Merchants Bureau's Tonghua, which arrived 12 hours late, and the Haiyan, which anchored to avoid fog off the coast of Wenzhou, delaying its entry by one day and rescheduled to arrive in Shanghai today. There was also the Sakimaru of the Dalian Steamship Company, which was also delayed outside Wusong for more than ten hours before arriving in the Huangpu River yesterday morning. In addition, ships such as the Jiujiang and Fusheng are expected to arrive in Shanghai today.

Stranded. The China Merchants Bureau's Tunan ship was stranded six miles downstream of Nanjing due to the sharp decline in the river water. It was not until yesterday when the morning tide rose that the ship was dragged out of the shoal. The ship has now sailed to Xiaguan and is scheduled to sail to Yingkou at 1:00 AM this morning.

Property Issues After the Merger of Trade Associations 110

The Receiving Issue Should Be the Responsibility of the Entire Reorganization Committee

The Method of Safekeeping, Use, and Management Should Be Handled Separately

The Shanghai Business Reorganization Committee replied to lawyer Tang Yingsong yesterday regarding the method of handling property after the merger of trade associations, stating that on the 17th of this month, they received a letter stating that after the merger of two trade associations, it was voluntarily agreed that the property should maintain its original state, and asking whether it conflicts with Article 10 of the reorganization and organization procedures set by the committee. It was submitted for discussion at the 43rd Standing Committee meeting of the committee on the 25th of this month, and it was decided that since the two groups have merged, all property should be received by the entire reorganization committee in accordance with the provisions of Article 10. However, if the reorganization committee or the general meeting of members decides on another method for the method of safekeeping, use, and management of the property, it can also be handled in accordance with its decision. This special record is hereby made in reply for your information.

Japanese Telegraph Office Increases Prices 113

The Japanese Telegraph Office in Shanghai has increased the price of telegrams to Japan from April 1st due to the sharp fall in the price of silver. Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Brain Membrane Inflammation Prevention 114

The Chief Medical Officer Formulates Five Measures

The Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Bureau, fearing the spread of brain membrane inflammation, has had its Chief Medical Officer formulate five preventive measures as follows: (1) Instruct all hygiene inspectors, train ticket inspectors, and station inspectors to pay special attention to patients infected with the disease. (2) Passengers with infectious diseases or suspected infectious diseases are not allowed to board the train without the permission of the Railway Bureau. (3) If a patient with an infectious disease or a suspected patient, or a corpse that died from the disease, is discovered during the journey, the patient or corpse should be immediately isolated to prevent infection, and the nearest medical office and the Chief Medical Officer should be immediately notified by telegram so that measures can be taken. (4) All vehicles in which infectious diseases or corpses of patients are found should be immediately sealed off, and passengers should be prohibited from entering or leaving. When arriving at the station, they should be unloaded, removed from the train, moved to a designated location, and thoroughly disinfected. (5) All personnel serving on the train who need mouthwash and anti-epidemic gauze masks can collect them from the medical offices.
