Local News 2

In the Vast Sea of Sin, a Young Man Drowns Himself 122

The Sinful Relationship in a Brothel

Results in Loss of Both Person and Money

Chen Baoshan's Repentant Words

Admonishing People Never to Patronize Prostitutes

The Anshan Maru, a small Japanese Osaka Company ferry, runs between the Puxi Wuma Road Bund and the Pudong Zhangjiabang Wharf. At around 5 p.m. the day before yesterday, the boat was on its way back to Pudong from Puxi. From the crowd of passengers, suddenly a young man jumped into the water to commit suicide. At that time the boat was moving quickly, and the waves were raging. The man instantly disappeared without a trace. The crew tried to save him but it was too late. The boat crew only found some belongings: a suicide note, a georgette jacket, a Central Bank 50-cent note, a five-cent airmail stamp, six copper coins, a small knife and several keys, and four pawn tickets. The items were temporarily collected by the crew and handed over to the Lujiazui Water Police for safekeeping when the ship returned to Puxi. They stated that the man had jumped into the river. The head of the police station ordered that the body be identified once it was recovered. The suicide note is recorded below (as it was, without edits) to reveal the reasons for the suicide:

To all gentlemen: Greetings. I used to work in a Westerner’s hotel. Last August, I met Zheng Meihong, a prostitute, at the Xinxin Garden, who lived at No. 243 Yulin Lane, Guling Road in the British Concession. Meihong and I fell in love deeply. By the end of the year, I had spent thousands of dollars on her. Meihong wanted to be redeemed because she was suffering at home. I spoke to Zheng, the madam, and the madam said she wanted $450 to redeem her. I offered $300, but the madam refused, and there was nothing I could do. This spring, on the eighth day of the first month, Zhang Liansheng, a regular customer of Meihong, met Meihong at the Xinxin Garden. She told Liansheng that she had no customers at home and was suffering every day, and asked him to save her. Because Liansheng had a wife, he couldn’t do anything. Meihong told Liansheng that she had a customer working in a hotel and that he could call him and speak to him. Liansheng called me six times to meet her at the hotel. On the ninth day, I went to the hotel and listened to Meihong’s suffering. I decided to help her out of conscience. On the tenth night, I had Meihong stay at the hotel and asked Liansheng to speak to the madam. Because Meihong was suffering, she didn’t want to go home. She told the madam to tell me that she had a customer named Chen who would take her away and that she wanted to speak to me at the hotel. The madam came to the hotel and said that Meihong didn’t want to go home and that she could go wherever she wanted. I thought that if something untoward happened, how could I live in this world with peace of mind? So I said that I would pay the same price as last year. The madam agreed immediately. On the eighteenth day, I paid her $150, with the remaining amount due on the eighth day of the second month. On the twentieth day of the first month, Meihong and I went to Hangzhou and stayed at the Qinghua Hotel. On the second night of the second month, I had to return to Shanghai for business and asked Meihong to stay in Hangzhou for a few days. When I returned to Shanghai, I lost my job, so I returned to Hangzhou on the third day. When I arrived at the hotel, Meihong was gone. I asked the tea attendant, who said that her family had taken her back. I immediately returned to Shanghai and asked the madam why she had taken Meihong back. The madam said that she had not returned to Shanghai and asked me who I was asking for. On the eighth day, the madam asked Hu Bingsheng, a gambler, to force me to sign a bond. I couldn’t bear it, so I signed a bond. Thinking about it, I had lost both the person and the money. I had lost my job, I had no money, and I had pawned all my clothes. I had no face to live in this world, so I jumped into the river to die. I hope all of you gentlemen will never patronize prostitutes. Written by Chen Baoshan from Shangyu County, aged 22, on March 25th.

The Case of the Customs Silver Box 123

A Silver Box Extra in the River Inspection Division

Moved from the Secretary's Office Next Door

The Box Surface Damaged by a Thief with a Saw

The Documents Inside the Box Were Not Lost

There was a case about a silver box in the office of the River Inspector Hallerman of the Jianghai Customs, Hankou Road, Bund, which was spied on by a thief. Fortunately, the box was very strong and was not broken. The contents of the box were various documents, not jewelry or treasures, so what was the use of it? This is a question. At present, the police authorities are secretly investigating. If the truth of this case is still unknown, it cannot be assumed. This incident was discovered on Thursday morning, the 27th of this week. The silver box was originally placed in the room of the secretary of Herr Hallerman, Gand. At about 6:30 a.m. that morning, the servant passed by the aisle and saw that the door was open and the silver box had been moved and transported to Hallerman's office. The surface of the silver box had been sawed by a thief. He was so shocked that he rushed to inform the person in charge of the customs and summoned the police to investigate. This case is quite bizarre, so the details are as follows:

The River Inspector Hallerman's office is on the fourth floor. There is a writing desk in the room, facing the entrance door. There is a convenient door on the left and a window on the right. Behind the window in the corner of the room is a large silver box. Next to it is a file cabinet for storing documents. Although the whole room is not very spacious, it is bright and clean, and the layout is well-organized. The office of Herr Hallerman's office is next door to his secretary Gand's residence. The two households are next to each other, and it is convenient to travel back and forth. The silver box that was lost was from Gand's room. Mr. Hallerman habitually leaves the office at about 4 o'clock every day after finishing his work. On the second day of the incident, that is, on Wednesday afternoon at about 4:30 p.m., he left his office and locked it. The next day, Thursday, the case of the silver box being attacked was discovered by the servant in the morning.

At about 6:30 a.m. this morning, a servant passed by the outside of Herr Hallerman's door. The double doors were open, and there was a silver box in the room. It was the one that had been moved from the opposite household. The box was about two and a half feet high and similar in width. It was black on the outside. The area around the lock handle of the box door was sawed open, but because the box was very strong, thick, and solid, it could not be sawed in, leaving only a deep mark. After the incident, the police station sent detectives to investigate, but they were unable to find any clues for a while. However, it was heard that the raincoat and mandarin jacket of a Chinese staff member in the aisle of the Tax Department office on the third floor below were also stolen. It is unknown whether it is related to the silver box case. All the things stored in the ill-fated silver box are documents, which are useless to ordinary people. After checking, nothing was lost. However, the police officers are convinced that the number of people engaged in this theft must be between three and five. As for what they intended to do, it is confusing and a dumb riddle in a hundred-foot-high building.

According to the Shanghai Times, it was rumored yesterday that three iron boxes in the office of Customs Patrol Inspector Hillman were pried open on Wednesday night and many valuable documents were lost. The office of the Patrol Inspector is in the Customs Building on the Bund. How could his iron box be pried open? The matter is quite strange and is currently under investigation. It is said that this matter may not have been done by an outside thief.

Local Merchants Angrily Assaulted 124

The Arrogance of the Thugs is Sky-High

Wang Xiaoxizi is Inadvertently Injured

The Garrison Headquarters dispatched several civil servants at 1 p.m. on the 16th of this month to search the Gonghe ship at the Yihua Wharf in Hongkou and seized a large amount of opium and unrefined opium. The local merchants had escaped in advance, so they were not caught. Afterwards, the local merchants suspected that Wang Daxizi, a Jiangbei native, had reported them. Wang was a salesman for the Gongxing Salt Shop on Chongyuanfang Road, and he went to various ships to sell salt due to his job. When the staff of the Garrison Headquarters boarded the Gonghe ship to search that day, Wang happened to be on the ship soliciting business. He was suspected because of this. After the searchers left, the local merchants instigated more than a dozen thugs to insult and scold Wang, and they were about to commit violence. Wang, fearing that he would be embarrassed, endured it and did not argue, and immediately returned to the store. However, the thugs did not give up, and they went to Gongxing. At the signal of the leader, wooden sticks and benches flew together, and Wang was pushed down and beaten. The salt shop immediately reported to the Hongkou Police Station, and detectives He Xiaozhi and Ding Yugao rushed to the scene. Wang had already been seriously injured. The two detectives arrested the two leading thugs, Xu Tianfu from Zhenjiang and Qian Changfa, a local, and the rest scattered. The injured were sent to the Tongren Hospital for treatment. Yesterday morning, the police sent the two criminals to the Provisional Court, and Judge Tan proposed to continue the trial. The lawyer for the plaintiff claimed that the injuries of the victim Wang Daxizi were very serious, his muscles and bones had been broken, and the internal injuries were even more severe. The hospital had scheduled an operation today, so the victim's life was in danger after the operation. Therefore, the victim came to court today with injuries and requested to be questioned first. Wang Daxizi then stated that the Gonghe ship was privately transporting opium and was searched by personnel from the Garrison Headquarters. I did not know about it, and I did not report it. Because I happened to be on the ship selling salt that day, I was unreasonably implicated. The thugs who committed the violence were all from the local merchant company. After being beaten, I have been receiving treatment until now, and I still cannot move my hands. At that time, the thugs beat me arbitrarily. Qian Changfa was also at the scene. Xu Tianfu slapped my face, and Tianfu's son, Xu Dagezi, was especially vicious and beat me the most. Then, the witness Wang Xiaosanzi testified that he had seen Xu Tianfu slap the plaintiff's face, and he had also seen Xu order the thugs to start beating him after slapping his face. When the defendant Xu Qian was questioned, the testimony was evasive. Lawyers Jiang Baoli and Fan Gang were hired to defend them. Judge Tan said that the defendants were heavily involved in the case and ordered Xu Tianfu to pay a bail of 1,000 yuan and Qian Changfa to pay a bail of 500 yuan for a retrial at a later date.

Four Cases of Sichuan Opium 125

French Police Detective Chief Shen Defu, Inspector Chen Sanlin, Detectives (?) Chen, Lu Yongxing, Mao Jinsheng, etc., seized four cases of Sichuan opium from the home of Chen Haosheng at No. 8 Zidelai Street, Li De Lane, who was secretly selling opium in violation of the ban. French Concession Police Solve 20,000 Yuan Robbery Case 126

Two Main Robbers Each Sentenced to Five Years in Prison

To Be Sent to Mainland Authorities for Further Trial

The Banque Franco-Chinoise branch at the east end of the Great World on Avenue Edward VII in the French Concession, on the morning of the 22nd of last month at approximately 8 a.m., ordered an old clerk to deliver banknotes and silver dollars totaling 20,000 yuan to a branch in the British Concession. As soon as he left the door, he was accosted by several robbers who displayed pistols to intimidate him, seizing all the silver dollars and fleeing. This was reported in a previous issue. Detectives Jin Jiulin, Wang Rusong, and Bao Tan Zhang Daorong of the special investigation unit of the French Concession Police investigated the whereabouts of the robbers and immediately arrested the robbers Xu Shungui, Zhou Bosong, female robber Qiu Zhou Shi, and Chen Li Shi, confiscating two pistols with bullets and 2,240 yuan in stolen silver dollars. They were brought to the police station. Later, suspects Shi Fengchang, Chen Xiaobing, and Cao Niao Ming were also apprehended. Yesterday, they were brought to the French court for questioning. Chen Zhiquan, the manager of the Banque Franco-Chinoise, filed a complaint, recounting the circumstances of the robbery. Subsequently, Western Detective Sergeant Salsil reported that the defendant Qiu Zhou Shi had previously been arrested for theft but was released after questioning due to lack of evidence. When she was apprehended this time, two pistols were found in her room, indicating that the robbers, fearing searches by police detectives, used women to carry pistols when committing robberies, requesting a severe inquiry. Under questioning, Xu Shungui confessed that he was from Shaoxing, lived at 1092 Tongchun Lane on Broadway Road, and had no occupation. Last month, while walking along Rue Louvain, he met a friend named Chen Fusheng, who invited him to a teahouse to talk about how to make a living. Chen said there was an opportunity to commit robbery and asked Xu to find people. Xu agreed and they parted. The next day, the 21st, Xu invited Zhou Bosong to meet Chen at the Dahua Apartments on Rue Paul Beau. Two people named Liu and Jin were already there. They went together to the entrance of the Great World and secretly waited. They saw the old clerk taking the silver out. Xu went home and waited until the next morning. He saw the old clerk carrying the banknotes out, and Chen Fusheng and Zhou Bosong, acting as lookouts, used weapons to intimidate the clerk and seize the banknotes, firing a shot into the sky as a warning before fleeing. Afterward, Chen Fusheng distributed more than 2,000 yuan in banknotes to Xu, who gave Zhou Bosong 40 yuan. Zhou Bosong's confession was the same. Qiu Zhou Shi confessed that she was a prostitute and had an affair with Xu Shungui for nine months. Chen Fusheng had left the pistols at her place for safekeeping. Chen Li Shi confessed that she had an affair with Chen Fusheng for only three months and did not know about the robbery. It is now unknown where Chen Fusheng has fled. Shi Fengchang, Chen Xiaobing, and Cao Niao Ming all confessed that they did not know Xu and were unaware of the robbery, requesting a clear investigation. Judge Zhu, after reading the police report and the defendants' confessions, which the defendants acknowledged, sentenced Xu Shungui and Zhou Bosong to five years in the Western jail each, to be deported and sent to mainland authorities for trial. Qiu Zhou Shi was sentenced to three years, to be deported permanently upon completion of her term. Chen Li Shi was to be deported permanently. Shi, Chen, and Cao were released due to lack of evidence. The stolen money was to be returned to the plaintiff, and the pistols were confiscated.

Film Censorship Committee Scheduled 128

To Censor Films in the Special District

Censorship to Begin on April 1st

The Municipal Film Censorship Committee, established by the Public Security, Social Affairs, and Education Bureaus based on the film censorship regulations promulgated by the Ministry of Interior and the Ministry of Education, has been censoring films screened in the Chinese area for five months. However, the committee, from its inception, had the goal of subjecting films in the special districts to the same censorship. Due to the special circumstances of the city, this could not be done simultaneously. After the "Fear Not Death" film incident, the committee felt that censoring the special districts could no longer be delayed. Therefore, it convened a temporary meeting on the 18th of this month, and invited representatives from the Municipal Propaganda Department to attend. It was decided that censoring films in the special districts would begin on April 1st. The measures are listed below: (1) Instruct all cinemas that, starting April 1st, film advertisements must state "This film has been approved for public screening by the Shanghai Municipal Film Censorship Committee." Films that have not been censored will not be allowed to be advertised. (2) The Municipal Party Headquarters and the Film Censorship Committee will send letters to all newspapers stating that, starting April 1st, film advertisements without the above statement should not be published. (3) If any film uses the phrase "has been censored" without actually having been censored, in addition to asking the newspaper to remove the advertisement the next day, the application to censor the film will not be accepted.

The department, considering the park to be public property, found it inconvenient to allow private individuals to conduct such business and rejected the application.

Municipal Government Approves 130

Amendment to the Route of the French Water Pipe Signal Line

The French Tramway and Electricity Company signed a contract with the Municipal Government on March 22 of last year to lay a No. 4 water pipe in the Chinese area. Article 2 of the contract stipulated that an electrical signal line could be laid along the water pipe to transmit the water level of the French Concession water towers and reservoirs to the Xiaojia Factory water plant. Now, the company stated that if the line followed the water pipe route exactly, it would have to cross the French Concession, taking the route of Rue Louvain, Rue Comte, Rue Luban, and then entering the factory, which would be a long route. If, at the intersection of Sanguantang Road and Lujiabang, it separated from the new water pipe and followed the existing No. 2 water pipe along Lujiabang Road, entering the French Concession at Xieqiao and going straight to the Lujiiawan General Factory via Xujiahui Road, it would shorten the length and save on road excavation work. They sent a letter to the Municipal Public Works Bureau asking for permission to change the route and stated that they were willing to bear all road excavation fees for digging Lujiabang Road. The bureau checked the request and found that, although it changed the terms of the contract, it was not without reason. Therefore, it sought the consent of the Land Bureau and the Public Works Bureau and jointly submitted it to the Municipal Government. It is now known that the Municipal Government has instructed that the approval be granted.

Murder of Stepmother Case Adjourned 132

Investigation of Reconciliation Records Required

A Monk and a Nun Must Appear in Court

The case of Zhang Wenqing, the daughter of a deceased official from Huzhou, colluding with Chen Hengcai, the son of her family's maid, and Yao Yonggui and Gao Jintang to kill her stepmother Zhang Su Shi has been widely publicized throughout Shanghai. The courtroom has been crowded for every hearing. The case had already concluded its arguments, and the final sentencing was originally scheduled for yesterday morning. Those concerned about the case all got up especially early yesterday and went to observe. At the ninth stroke of the bell, the second court of the Provisional Court was already full. Half an hour later, it felt even more crowded. Suddenly, Judge Luo Renji ascended to the bench and ordered the four defendants, Zhang Wenqing and others, to stand at the defendant's position. At this moment, the courtroom was silent and solemn, listening to this final five-minute judgment. Judge Luo then declared that the case was originally scheduled for sentencing today, but after examination, it was found that the reconciliation records of the deceased and the first wife in the lawsuit still needed to be investigated, so the judgment could not be announced today. Judge Luo then questioned Zhang Wenqing about the dharma name and address of the monk who participated in the reconciliation. Zhang confessed that there was a monk and a nun who mediated at the time, and the reconciliation record was made by the monk, whose name was Yushan, the abbot of Conglin Temple in Yangzhou, and the nun's name was Genshan, who lived at the Tongshan Hall on Carter Road in this city. He then briefly questioned Chen Hengcai and Gao Jintang a few more times, instructing them to be remanded into custody separately and to summon the two witnesses, Yushan and Genshan, to court on the afternoon of April 7 for cross-examination, and ordered a re-opening of arguments. The audience then dispersed, and the case will have to go through another round of arguments before a date for the final judgment can be set.

Record of the Trial of the Kidnapping of Brothers Case 133

Xi Xiangquan and Xi Xianglin

Shen Xinyi and Tan Xinglou

On September 22 of last year, a bizarre kidnapping case occurred in Nanhui County. Xi Xiangquan, a wealthy landowner, was kidnapped and later released for a ransom of 7,000 yuan. The case implicated college student Shen Xinyi, his brother-in-law Tan Xinglou, and Xi Xiangquan's elder brother Xi Xianglin, who were arrested by the county public security bureau and subjected to torture. Shen and others refused to accept this and filed complaints with the provincial government's civil affairs department, the high court, and the judicial yuan, accusing the former Nanhui County magistrate Shen Zhizhong of illegal dereliction of duty and the former public security bureau chief Cao Yongqi of abusing torture. The high court then assigned the Shanghai District Court to investigate and handle the case. A trial was held but not concluded. Yesterday morning, Judge Qian convened another hearing. First, the kidnapped person Xi Xiangquan testified that on the night of September 22 last year, he suddenly heard Tan Xinglou calling at the door. At that time, I had already turned off the lights and was sleeping in the accounting room. I put on my clothes and went out to see about twenty people, each holding a pistol and a flashlight, who dragged me to the field corner and blindfolded me. (Question) Do you know Shen Xinyi? (Answer) I don't know him, but Tan Xinglou often comes to my house. Next, Xi's mother, Xi Yangshi, testified that Xianglin and Xiangquan are both my sons. I am deaf and blind. When Xiangquan was kidnapped, I was pressed to the ground by a group of people and covered with a quilt, unable to call for help. Then, the witness Xi Taoran testified that Xi Xianglin was indeed eating wedding banquet at my house on the night of September 21 last year. On September 23, people from their family came to my house to report that Xiangquan had been kidnapped. Then, on September 24, Xianglin went back. Under questioning, the defendants Shen Xinyi, Tan Xinglou, and Xi Xianglin all denied the charges. Tan Xinglou testified that I had eaten at Xiangquan's house three times after Xiangquan was released. Shen Xinyi also said that in September last year, I was teaching in Kaifeng, Henan, introduced by a friend named Xu. I request that Xu be summoned to court to provide evidence. At this point, the lawyer Wang Zengxian, hired by Xi Xianglin, made a statement. The judge ordered that another joint trial be held later. Shen Xinyi and Tan Xinglou were remanded into custody, and Xi Xianglin remained on bail. The court then adjourned.

Dispute Among Foremen at the Wusong River Customs Station 135

Crowd of Flagmen Submits Document to Customs Commissioner

Zhou Linhe, the Chinese chief foreman of the Zhang Huabang River Customs Station in Songnan, resigned after his term of service expired. According to precedent, the vacant position should have been filled by the second foreman, Yin Yunlang, and the vacant second foreman position should have been filled by Song Yinlang, who has served the longest. However, the foreign officer in charge of the station promoted Zhou Adi, who has not yet served fifteen years, instead, causing dissatisfaction among the flagmen at Fort Baoshan. They submitted a document to the Shanghai Customs and River Affairs Commissioners, requesting a thorough investigation and handling of the matter. It is heard that the Customs Commissioner has sent a letter to the foreign officer at Zhang Huabang, instructing the foremen to go to Shanghai for an interview. The original document is transcribed below: To falsely report to superiors, disrupt regulations, and promote foremen improperly, requesting a thorough investigation. Respectfully reporting, we, the undersigned flagmen at Fort Baoshan, because the Zhang Huabang flag chief foreman (Na Ma Hun) Zhou Linhe has completed his term of service and has requested to resign, which has been approved, and will hand over the position on April 1. The vacant chief foreman position should be filled by the Fort Baoshan second foreman (Na Ma Tuo) Ba Yuang. The vacant second foreman position, according to customs regulations, should be filled by Song Yinlang, who has served the longest. Unexpectedly, Zhou Linhe, by fraudulent means, and with the Zhang Huabang Deputy River Affairs Commissioner, promoted his nephew Zhou Adi, who has the shortest seniority and lacks experience as an inspector, ahead of others. It is rumored that this has already been decided. We believe that this matter concerns fairness and violates regulations. We have specifically clarified the facts. The reason is that Zhou Linhe only knows how to benefit himself, disregards justice, and imitates the feudal power of warlords, occupying all foreman positions for the Zhou family and not allowing others to intervene. Now, the newly promoted Na Ma Hun Yin Yunlang is Linhe's brother-in-law, and the small steamship captain Zhou Linlin is his elder brother. However, the vacant Na Ma Tuo position is not considering promoting Song Yinlang, who has served for 28 or 29 years, but is instead promoting his nephew Zhou Adi, who has not yet served fifteen years, ahead of others, treating regulations as trifles and justice as child's play. Under the banner of the Blue Sky White Sun, he still wants to use feudal power to suppress colleagues, making it impossible for others to be promoted, which is not allowed by law and is difficult for justice to tolerate. We believe that this matter concerns the public and cannot be tolerated in silence. Therefore, we have no choice but to briefly describe the facts and earnestly request a thorough investigation and handling to uphold justice and comply with regulations. We urgently submit this report and await your orders. Respectfully submitted by the flagmen at Fort Baoshan.

Commodity Inspection Bureau 136

Publishes International Trade Guide

First Issue Scheduled for Publication on April 1

The Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce believes that inspecting export commodities is for the purpose of developing foreign trade. In addition to inspection duties, it also has the important responsibility of improving domestic commodities and developing foreign trade. The director of the bureau, Youyan, has specially a monthly publication, named International Trade Guide. The content is divided into reviews, research, statistics, domestic and foreign industrial and commercial news, and inspection policy news, etc., specifically containing important articles on industry and commerce and international trade. It is now heard that the first issue has been printed and is scheduled for publication on April 1. In addition to Director Zou's Export Commodity Inspection: Purpose and Method, and a detailed list of Chinese and foreign inspection policies, there are several important articles, such as China's Egg Product Export Trade, An Observation of the History of China's Silk Trade from a Statistical Perspective, and Cotton Inspection Policy, all of which are over 10,000 words long. The statistics and industrial and commercial news are also very valuable reference materials. The price is three yuan per year and three jiao per issue. In order to facilitate foreign merchants' understanding of China's export commodity situation, the bureau also publishes a monthly commodity inspection bulletin in English, named Export Inspection Bulletin, which specifically contains details on export commodities. It is also scheduled for publication on April 1. The price is four yuan per year and four jiao per issue. These two monthly publications in Chinese and English are available from the bureau's office at No. 15 Museum Road, as well as from the branch libraries of the Commercial Press and the China Book Company in various provinces.

Rice Boat Robbed En Route 138

Half a Cargo of White Rice Taken by Those Claiming to Be Refugees

Zhang Songgen's rice boat from Qingjiao, loaded with 150 shi of white rice, was en route to Shanghai the day before yesterday. Because the wind was unfavorable, it anchored at the border of Qingjiao. Suddenly, more than 20 Jiangbei small boats arrived, with a large number of people, claiming to be refugees, men, women, and children, swarming onto the boat. They opened Zhang's boat's cargo hold and, seeing the rice, claimed they were borrowing it. Zhang told the refugees that this was cargo for customers and could not be lent out. He said that if they were short of food, he would be responsible. His attempts to stop them were ineffective, and they used baskets to carry away approximately half of the cargo. Fortunately, a customs patrol boat, after being notified, sped to the scene to suppress the situation, but the boats had already escaped. Zhang came to Shanghai yesterday to report to rice merchant Wang. Rice boats in Shanghai were alarmed upon hearing the news and were wary. It is reported that rice merchants will hold a meeting to discuss prevention measures.

A Pair of Unhappy Lovers at the Xinzao Bridgehead 139

Dong A'tu Meets His Runaway Wife on the Road

Wu Xiaomei Doesn't Want to Go Home

Yesterday afternoon at approximately 5 p.m., a young, short-haired, fashionable woman was weeping loudly by the river at the Xinzao Bridgehead on Xinzao Road. In an instant, onlookers crowded around. Suddenly, a man resembling a country bumpkin pushed through the crowd and grabbed the woman. After a while, five or six ruffians came and forced her to go to the Chunjiang Teahouse. According to the country bumpkin, his name is Dong A'tu, from Chongming. The woman's name is Wu Xiaomei, 18 years old, and she is his wife. They were married in their hometown last autumn and were initially harmonious. However, she disliked my ugly appearance and her feelings gradually faded. I knew I was not attractive to women, so when I married her, I did it entirely with money. I gave her parents 500 yuan and paid off her debts of more than 300 yuan. However, after three days, she treated me like an enemy and never let me touch her. I knew my shortcomings and was accommodating in every way. Unexpectedly, she took an inch and wanted a mile, taking my ornaments and running away to Shanghai. It's been two months. The day before yesterday, I was informed by a friend and came to Shanghai to look for her. I met her on Datong Road and she had completely changed her appearance. I urged her to return home, but not only did she refuse, but she also denied that I was her husband. So I wanted to take her to the police station. According to the woman, my parents were blinded by greed. Because he was rich, they sacrificed me, a small and weak woman, for him to trample on. I was raped when I was fourteen. He used his money and power to marry me, but he is nearly forty years old and has a hidden disease. There is no marital joy at all, so I eloped to Shanghai. Now I am a maid in North Sichuan Road. If he wants me to return home and resume our marriage, I would rather drown myself in the river. Later, the Shanghai ruffians forced the woman into a pre-hired car, which sped off in the direction of Carter Road. The woman was still crying all the way.

Golden Wu's Suicide Attempt in the River: 141

Because Jin Minggui was Having an Affair

Jin Minggui from Ningbo is a lacquer craftsman who lives at the fourth house in Changxing Lane, Yuezhou Road, Hongkou. His wife, Wu, is 29 years old, also from Ningbo. Recently, because Jin was having an affair with another woman outside, he insisted that Wu move back to their hometown, claiming it was to save expenses. However, Wu was unwilling to return, leading to disagreements. Yesterday morning at 8:00 AM, she went to the Dongyang Wharf and attempted to drown herself in the river. She was rescued by Officer No. 316, who took her to Tongren Hospital for treatment.

Female Corpse Found on Dinghai Road 142

Around 6:20 AM yesterday morning, a female corpse was discovered on an open space on Dinghai Road, Yangshupu. The Yangshupu Police Station dispatched detectives to investigate. The deceased appeared to be from a middle-class family.

Strange News of a Stolen Antique Porcelain Vase 143

Stolen Suddenly, Gone Swiftly

Zhang Juncheng's Home Fortunate to Avoid Robbery

At the home of Zhang Juncheng, No. 44, Old Shanghai County Houjie (Back Street), Shanghai, at around 2:00 AM the night before last, a robber suddenly appeared. He descended from the roof of a neighboring house using a rope and broke into the upstairs inner room. Holding a gun, he threatened the occupants to remain silent. He robbed them of tens of dollars in cash and some miscellaneous jewelry. Still unsatisfied, he forced the owner to open the lock on the chest. Unexpectedly, two bullets from the pistol held by the robber fell to the ground. As the robber bent down to pick up the bullets, the owner seized the opportunity to grab the robber's pistol. Shouting for help, they struggled with each other, causing antique porcelain vases and other items to fall onto the floor below, making a loud noise. People downstairs were awakened and began shouting to catch the thief. The robber then forcefully pushed the owner down, jumped out of the window, climbed over the roof of the side room, and escaped from the roof of Fumei Lane. During the struggle with the robber, the owner suffered injuries with bleeding to the hairline of his right ear and both hands. The incident has been reported to the First District Second Precinct for investigation.

Boatman Involved in Kidnapping Case 144

Firearms Found on the Boat

He Shaoqing from Xuzhou, 32 years old, makes a living as a boatman. He spends his nights on his boat at Lujiazui, Pudong. Yesterday at noon, Detectives Mao Yiwen from the Shanghai Municipal Council Public Security Bureau, along with Western detectives from the Hongkou Police Station, suddenly arrived armed and took a boat to Lujiazui to arrest He. Seeing the situation, He panicked and quickly rowed the boat to the Fenshan Wharf ferry, attempting to flee ashore. He was spotted by the patrol officer at the ferry, who found his behavior suspicious. He was taken to the Fourth Team of the Lujiazhai Police Station. At the same time, the detectives also tracked him to the team. The team leader dispatched senior officers to search the boat, where they found 41 pistol bullets and a magazine. They were all brought to the team. Team Leader Zhu questioned He briefly and then sent him to the Third District Office of the Public Security Bureau, which transferred him to the Public Security Bureau for further action. It is rumored that He is involved in a certain kidnapping case, so the police ordered detectives to secretly arrest him. His boat has been impounded by the First Squad of the Lujiazui Water Patrol and is awaiting disposal by the headquarters.

Robbery Solved Immediately 145

At the Home of Wu Qian in South Chengdu Road

At the home of Mrs. Wu Qian, No. 705 South Chengdu Road, just after finishing lunch the day before yesterday, four robbers suddenly appeared. They pulled out pistols and threatened the occupants to remain silent. They robbed two chests of clothes and gold and silver jewelry, worth a total of one thousand dollars, and fled with the stolen goods. Zhang Zhongda from Changzhou, the thief carrying the two chests, was seen by two Chinese constables, No. 2040 and No. 2242, midway through the escape. Suspecting his behavior, they arrested him and took him to the Xinzha Police Station. The thief confessed everything freely and provided information that their base was located at Room 33, Yunzhou Hotel, North Hai Road. Detectives Zhang Ankang and Tao Rubo were secretly dispatched to arrest accomplices Yang A'er (nicknamed "Little Hubei") from Hubei Province and Zhang Jinfao from Pudong. Two pistols with live ammunition were found. Yesterday morning, along with Zhang Zhongda, they were all brought to the Provisional Court. Judge Luo interrogated them and ordered them to be detained for further investigation and trial at a later date.

Arrest of Hoodlums in Pudong 146

Regarding the Shi Chunsheng Robbery Case

Jin Mao Escapes, Zhang Shaoyun Captured

About two or three miles northeast of Gaoqiao Town in Pudong, at the intersection of the three counties of Shanghai, Baoshan, and Chuansha, there is a river called Jiebang. The area south of the bridge is under the jurisdiction of the first district of Shanghai County. Nearby lives Shi Chunsheng, who used to work at the Wuhu Customs and has a comfortable family situation, making him a target of criminal gangs. Zhang Shaoyun (nicknamed "Xiao Guangdan"), a well-known hoodlum in Gaoqiao Town, specializes in creating trouble and exploiting the local people in the countryside. His son, Jin [illegible character], relies on his father's reputation as a hoodlum and forms gangs, acting lawlessly in the countryside. Recently, they learned that the Shi family had considerable savings, so they gathered a gang, armed themselves, and went to rob Shi's home. Because they were unfamiliar with the route, they temporarily forced a local tailor, Mr. Jia, to act as their guide. They went to Shi's home and robbed him of several hundred dollars' worth of property. Still not satisfied, they also robbed the neighboring Zhu family and another family. They fled with the loot, divided it, and spent it. Shi Chunsheng recognized Mr. Jia among the robbers, so he immediately reported to the Fourth Precinct of the Third District. Precinct Chief Lan Zhusan dispatched police to arrest the tailor, Mr. Jia, who confessed that Zhang Jinmao had organized the robbery. Because Zhang's family had been hoodlums for generations with many accomplices and possessed several pistols, Chief Lan immediately reported the situation to Director Yuan of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, who ordered the detective team to select capable detectives Gao Wansheng and Wang Chenglong, etc., to carry live ammunition pistols and rush to Gaoqiao Town across the river on the morning of the day before yesterday. They cooperated with the armed police officers of the precinct to arrest Zhang Shaoyun at his home in Jiangjiazhai. However, Jin Mao was well-informed and had already escaped. Only a pistol and a list of accomplices were found under the floor of the house. Later, Zhang Shaoyun was arrested at the Xujaqiao Teahouse and was sent to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for interrogation yesterday.

Minor Worker Injured in Fall During Repair of Diplomatic Building 147

Only Known by the Surname Zhao, Name Unknown

Chen Shiguang, Director of the Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, after receiving orders to take over the former Jiangsu Special Envoy's Office building, moved the office into the building. However, the building had been neglected for years, resulting in several major leaks in the terrace during rainy weather. If repairs were not carried out quickly, the building would fall into disrepair. He submitted a request to Minister Wang for funds to repair the building, which was approved. The project was contracted to Yuanhe Foreign Firm with an estimated cost of several thousand taels. However, yesterday (the 28th) at 4:30 PM, a worker surnamed Zhao was working on the bituminous felt roofing on the clock tower of the diplomatic building. He accidentally stepped on the hatch under the bell. Because the hatch was not bolted, he lost his footing and fell, landing on the offering table in front of the portrait of Sun Yat-sen. Due to the height and weight, the surface of the offering table was broken, and the frame of Sun Yat-sen's portrait was also knocked down. He immediately lost consciousness. Although other workers tried to rescue him, he did not speak. The foreman immediately took him to Guangci Hospital for treatment. It is reported that he was seriously injured and still unable to speak, so the worker's name could not be determined. According to the foreman, the bituminous felt roofing project was contracted to Dayouyi Hardware Store. The injured worker was temporarily hired, so only his surname Zhao was known.

Verdict in the Case of a Japanese Girl Killed by a Car 148

An eight-year-old Japanese girl, Shi Qiangmaila, was hit and killed by a cargo truck with license plate number 16542, driven by a car driver named Cheng Atao, on Gordon Road. The police have filed a lawsuit against the car driver in the Provisional Court. As previously reported, the deceased girl lived in a foreign house at No. 967 Gordon Road and studied at a Japanese school. Every day, she was transported to and from school by car number 5339 arranged by her family. On the afternoon of the 13th of this month, the deceased and several other Japanese children were riding in the car back home. When the car arrived at the entrance of the residence, the children got out of the car one after another to return home. At that moment, Cheng Atao drove the cargo truck, knocking down and running over the girl. Although she was immediately taken to Fumin Hospital, it was too late to save her. She died from her injuries. The police accused Cheng of driving too fast, causing the fatal accident. After Judge Sun Yuan conducted a preliminary investigation, he determined that it was necessary to conduct an on-site investigation of the distance between where the deceased was hit and the roadside curb, as well as the circumstances at the time of the collision, the width of the road, and the direction of travel. Therefore, at 4:00 PM the day before yesterday, he went to the scene of the accident with the court clerk, the police lawyer Ru Baozhen, and the Western police chief Jefferson from the Gordon Road Police Station to conduct an on-site inspection. He also instructed the surveyor who went with them to make a detailed measurement of the site and create a map for reference. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Sun opened the Fifth Tribunal and ordered the defendant to be brought to court. After a brief interrogation, he immediately announced the verdict. The main text of the verdict stated that the defendant Cheng Atao was sentenced to one year of imprisonment for causing death due to negligence in the course of his business. The number of days of detention before the verdict was finalized was allowed to offset the imprisonment at a rate of two days per day.

Board Meeting of the Vagrant Work Relief Center Held Yesterday 149

The Shanghai Charity Association's Vagrant Work Relief Center held its tenth regular board meeting at Tongren Fuyuantang yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM. Nine directors attended. Wang Yiting presided over the meeting. (1) Director's report: (1) The Social Bureau forwarded the Public Security Department's subsidy for the charity expenses of the temple in the amount of 750 yuan per year. The first installment of 250 yuan has been received. (2) There are too many patients at the center, so a hospital has been opened. All seriously ill people are being treated in the hospital. (3) The current number of people working is 214. The weaving department has been opened. Merchants provide their own machines and raw materials to teach the inmates how to work. (4) The expenses for February were 3,435.01 yuan, which is 911.31 yuan less than the expenses for January. (2) Discussion: (1) The center signed a contract with Changji Cloth Factory. A resolution was passed to approve the contract with amendments. (2) The dormitory windows only have one side, so the air cannot circulate. It is not suitable for summer. What should be done? The resolution was passed for Director Zhang Xiaoliang to investigate. (3) Previous discussions were held about purchasing land in the prison cemetery for exchange, and Director Yang contacted the relevant parties once. Now the prison has reported to the ministry for review. Should it be handled according to the previous discussion? The resolution was passed to continue with the previous discussion and ask Director Yang to discuss the matter with the director of the prison. (4) The proposed budget for the center's income and expenses for the 19th year was submitted for review. The resolution was passed to submit it to the Charity Association for review and compilation. (5) [Omitted] The meeting adjourned after the discussions.

Ningbo Girl Yin Azhu Gets Lost in Hankou 150

After questioning her, she said that she is eleven years old, from Ningbo, and was abducted to Hankou. She got separated from her companion and got lost. She has parents who live in the French Concession of Shanghai. We should try to reunite her with her parents. We have sent Yin Azhu to the Hankou Women and Children's Relief Center for temporary shelter. We have also sent a letter to the Ningbo Public Security Bureau to find her family. We are sending a photo to your bureau for posting and publishing in the newspaper to find her family and uphold humanitarian principles. Please reply." A photo was enclosed. (See British Admiralty Chart No. 362). All ships are hereby notified to pay close attention and remember this to avoid negligence.

(1) Games Flag, (2) Military Band (3) All Staff and Referees of the Games (4) Staff and Athletes from Various Provinces, Cities, and Districts (In order of receipt of the list, with staff first, women next, and men last) (1) Hubei Province, (2) Guangdong Province, (3) Hong Kong, Qingdao City, (5) Anhui Province, (6) Jiangxi Province (7) Suiyuan (8) Liaoning Province, (9) Fujian Province (10) Hunan Province, (11) East Special District (12) Beijing City, (13) Tianjin City, (14) Shanxi Province, (15) Kobe, (16) Nanjing City, (17) Henan Province, (18) Jiangsu Province, (19) Shanghai City, (20) Sichuan Province, (21) Shandong Province, (22) Hebei Province, (23) Shaanxi Province, (24) Zhejiang Province, (25) All Students Performing from Hangzhou Elementary Schools The route is as follows: All staff and athletes will assemble in front of the dormitory at 8:30 AM and line up in four columns in the order listed above. The games flag will lead the way out of the office building, heading east to the main entrance of the stadium, turning west into the track and field, circling the field once, and then entering the runway to the designated location, facing the podium in order. (3) Oath Ceremony

Each unit will hold its unit's flag and lead the team leaders forward to the runway, facing the podium. They will read the oath aloud. All athletes will read aloud in response. At this time, the team leader will tilt the team flag halfway and raise it in salute.

Hong Kong Chinese Football Team Wins the International Cup 167

Result: Crushing Defeat of Scotland by Five to Zero

Past Records: Hong Kong, 23rd – This is the sixth International Charity Competition since its inception in Hong Kong. In the past five sessions, apart from the first, a total of four teams have participated in each session: the Chinese team, the British team, the Scottish team, and the Portuguese team. The Portuguese team joined in the second session. Over the past five years, Scotland has won three times, the British team once, and Portugal also managed to win once in their first year of participation. Looking back at our country, we have unfortunately failed in the finals every year. This victory, which can indirectly bring international honor through football, has been regrettably taken by others in each session.

This Year's Competition: This year, the four teams participating in the competition are still China, Britain, Scotland, and Portugal. In the preliminary rounds, Britain played against Scotland, and China played against Portugal. Among the four teams, China and Britain are the strongest. As a result, China defeated Portugal without saying. However, Scotland luckily defeated Britain. Therefore, the final match was between China and Scotland. The Scottish team was originally not weak, but unfortunately, many of their skilled players had been transferred to India not long ago. Therefore, the Scottish team lamented the difficulty in selecting talents. After recent consultations, a not-so-strong team was finally determined. Our country's army, on the other hand, is full of talent and does not worry about not having one. Everyone knows that this year has great potential. Yesterday, the long-awaited final between China and Scotland was held. This day was the second day of special horse racing. The weather was clear and sunny, and there were naturally many people going out. However, the number of people going to the football field to watch this final was several times more than those going to the racecourse to watch horse racing. Around three o'clock, the stands on the east and west sides were already packed with people. Those who arrived later continued to pour in like a tide. As a result, all the seats were occupied, and it was inevitably crowded and bustling, as one can imagine.

Lineup: Soon after, the Scottish army also arrived. Our country's army was wearing red and white striped jerseys and white pants, while the Scottish army wore blue jerseys and white pants, with blue and white socks. The flags of both sides were distinct, and the atmosphere was heroic. After taking photos together, the referee, Ya Qianchen, blew the whistle. Lin Yuying, the commander-in-chief of the Chinese army, and Valentime, the commander-in-chief of the Scottish army, met each other first, and then the battle began. The lineups of the two countries are as follows:

(China): Chen Xipei (Zhonghua), Li Yuda (Zhonghua), Li Tiansheng (Nanhua)

Lin Yuying (Zhonghua), Huang Ruihua (Zhonghua), He Zuoxian (Zhonghua)

Ye Beihua (Nanhua), Sun Jinshun (Zhonghua), Huang Baisong (Zhonghua), Li Huiguan (Zhonghua), Cao Guicheng (Zhonghua)

(Scotland): Luo Zha (Hong Kong Club), Ke Lin (Police), Shi Jilu Fei (Kowloon)

Mai Bulai (Hong Kong), Mai Jiliwei (Police), Jilu Qilai Shi (Hong Kong)

Shi Ge (Hong Kong), Valentime (Police), Fu Lisha (Police), Suobei (Navy), Bei Lu (Hong Kong)

Kickoff: The Scottish army got the advantage of the terrain first, and our army opened fire. Sun Tuitui kicked the ball to Ye Beihua, wanting to directly approach the Scottish capital along the left wing, but the right guard, Mai Jilu Fei, had strong legs and resisted the attack. The Scottish army immediately took advantage of the situation and forced back from the right wing, but it was ineffective. At this time, the momentum was strong, the firepower was fierce, and the bombs kept exploding, making the battlefield atmosphere extremely tense. Ye, the left wing forward of our team, advanced alone, firing three shots, but the Scottish army's defenses were strict and he could not succeed. Once, Cao, the right wing forward, rushed forward bravely and passed the ball to the center, but Huang and Sun missed the opportunity to cooperate.

One Goal: After a fierce battle, neither side could determine the winner. After about a hundred rounds of fighting, our army finally gained the upper hand. Not long after, Cao ran quickly on the right wing and passed the ball to a key area of the Scottish side. At this time, the veteran Huang Tuitui also arrived. The veteran did not covet the credit. Seeing the ball falling, he deliberately jumped high, intending to let Lao Sun take the shot. General Sun Tuitui was indeed a veteran of hundreds of battles. He intercepted the ball and shot again. The ball was neither high nor low, as fast as an arrow, and went straight to the enemy's goal. How could the Scottish goalkeeper, Luo Zha, resist it? Just like smoke passing before the eyes, the ball had already reached the bottom of the net. Our army won the first victory. Until the end of the first half, Cao shot another goal on the right wing, but the game was called to a halt. Although China scored twice in the first half, only one goal was counted as a victory.

Resume Battle: After exchanging positions, the Scottish army saw that the previous strategy was not effective and changed the lineup. Center Forward Fu Lisha retreated to become the right back, Mai Jilu Fei was changed to the center back, and Mai Jiliwei was moved to the center forward. The Scottish army beat the drums and opened fire first, wanting to regain the city, but our army was strong and the cannons were powerful. Not only did they defeat them, but they also continued to press forward. How could the Scottish army stand against our mighty army?

Two and Three: Another opportunity for our army arrived. Cao, on the right wing, took the corner kick. A certain general received the shot, hitting the top of the goalpost and bouncing to the ground. Originally, this shot would have entered the enemy's goal, but it was not counted. However, luckily, the veteran Huang got the ball and headed it. General Tuitui responded with another header, finally scoring. Our army won the second goal. Not long after, Ye rushed in sharply on the left wing. Fu Lisha tried to seize the ball, all the way to the boundary, but Ye got it back. He lightly passed it to Lao Sun, who shot with his left foot, but it was blocked. Unexpectedly, his right foot kicked up, and the ball went into the net again. Sun Tuitui scored for the third time.

Four and Five: Three victories for the Chinese team were not enough. Sun and Ye, the left and right wings, advanced each other. Ye passed to the right, and Cao went for a kick, but unfortunately, it went over the enemy's goal. Afterwards, the veteran Huang passed the ball to Cao on the right wing again. Cao passed it to the center, and the unlucky Fu Lisha touched the ball with his hand, receiving a penalty kick from the nearest position, a twelve-yard kick. Lin Yuying took the shot, and Luo Zha blocked it, but Lin kicked it again, scoring another victory. There was also the final victory, which was also shot in from the left wing by the veteran Huang. Until the end of the game, the Chinese team defeated the Scottish army by a score of five to zero, causing them to abandon their armor and retreat. In this battle, China defeated Scotland by a large margin and set a new record for overseas Chinese in Hong Kong.

Award Ceremony: After the bloody battle, the infinitely glorious International Cup had long been displayed at the entrance. At this time, the crowd of spectators gathered around to watch the excitement. First, the secretary of the Football Association, Holan Shi, gave a speech. Because our countrymen were too happy, his words were drowned out, and we only heard one sentence: "China has won for the first time this time." After the speech, Mrs. Su Xuke, representing the Chinese, awarded the cup to Lin Yuying. The commander-in-chief shouted a command, and the generals dispersed with three cheers.

Art Review: Judging the event based on the event, the Chinese team broke the ground this time to set a record for the Chinese and gain infinite glory internationally. In terms of merit-based awards, General Sun Tuitui made the greatest contribution. However, the eleven players who worked together to win each had special honors. Chen, the goalkeeper, insisted on not letting a few people succeed. Li and Li were brave in killing the enemy. The three central defenders assisted in attacking and defending without flaws. The forwards completed their tasks in one go, which is even more commendable. As for the Scottish army, the worst was Fu Lisha, who must take responsibility for the two goals lost. Mai Jiliwei and others had mediocre performances. Ke Lin was quite commendable, and Bei Lu and others had exhausted their abilities.

Epilogue: The Chinese team added infinite glory to China yesterday. The eleven players who played yesterday certainly deserve our praise. However, I believe that the members who defeated Portugal by three to zero in the preliminary round should also be recorded again to commemorate their merits. I remember that the people who played at that time were goalkeeper Bao Jiaping, defenders Wu Jinquan and Li Tiansheng, center backs Liang Rongde, Huang Ruihua, and Lin Yuying, and forwards Cao Guicheng, Chen Shaokang, Feng Jingxiang, Ye Beihua, and Chen Guangyao. Without the first victory, there would be no second victory yesterday. To commemorate their contributions, the two Chinese associations should reward them both together. The members who played fully in the previous match and did not participate again yesterday, I hope you remember them!

Ministry of Education Issues Order: Public Training Program During the Tutelage Period 171

The Third Plenary Session of the Central Committee passed the Public Training Program during the Tutelage Period, which was communicated to the Ministry of Education by the Executive Yuan. The Ministry of Education is now transmitting the original text of the program to the education administrative organs of various provinces and cities, as follows:

In order to remedy the shortcomings of past public movements, the Third National Congress of our Party resolved to establish the following four principles as the overall direction of future public movements:

(1) Public movements must be based on the needs of the people for social survival and create organized people.

(2) For national farmers and workers who already have considerable organization, our Party must assist them in the future to enhance their knowledge and skills, raise the standard of their social morality, and promote their productivity and output, so as to achieve the goal of improving the people's livelihood.

(3) Agricultural economy occupies the main part of China's national economy. Future public movements must support rural education, rural organizations, cooperative movements, and the dissemination of new agricultural production methods as the main tasks.

(4) Our Party should make every effort to create self-governing life within schools for young men and women in the future, implement universal physical training for young men and women, promote scientific and artistic gatherings, associations, and publications, and reward practical scientific research and inventions.

Fujian Volleyball Team 172

(Photographed by Mr. Lin Zemin)

In order to realize the above-mentioned principles and complete the work of tutelage, a public training program is formulated, divided into four sections: 1. Basic principles of public training; 2. Organization; 3. Training; 4. Responsibilities of Party departments and the government towards people's organizations. In the period of tutelage, we must implement the principles of public movement resolved by the Third National Congress. There are also things that should be determined in theory. Therefore, the first section stipulates the spirit of people's organization and the key points to be paid attention to in training. Secondly, to train the people, we must enable the people to have a sound organization, and then the progress of the training work will be effective. Therefore, the second section stipulates how the Party departments in various places should guide the organization of people's organizations. The scope of training, the methods and methods of training are stipulated in the third section. Moreover, in the past, the responsibilities of the Party departments and the government in various places towards people's organizations were unclear, which hindered the progress of the public movement work. Therefore, the fourth section specifies the powers and responsibilities of the Party departments and the government towards people's organizations. This program is based on the needs of the tutelage period as a principle, and how to implement it should be handed over to the Central Standing Committee to formulate detailed methods based on this program for implementation.

Section 1: Basic Principles of Public Training

(1) The organization of people's groups is based on the principle of voluntary organization. (2) Training the people must recognize the needs of the people for social survival and the spirit of Party tutelage.

Section 2: Organization

(1) The Party department should guide various people's organizations to become sound organizations. (2) The Party department should guide various people to complete their organization.

Section 3: Training

First Item: Scope of Training (1) General Training A. Organizational Training: To enable the people to understand the meaning and methods of organization. B. Ideological Training: To enable the people to have a deep and definite understanding and belief in Party principles, and to understand the errors of the Communist Party in advocating class struggle, and to thoroughly understand the direction of public movement during the tutelage period. C. Behavioral Training: To make the people's actions conform to Party principles and to practice the construction work of the Three Principles of the People. (2) Special Training A. Business Knowledge Training: To enable the people to enrich their knowledge of business and understand their tasks for the country and society. B. Business Skills Training: To enable the people to improve their skills in business and promote the development of construction undertakings.

Second Item: Training Methods (1) Grouping: Divide the members of each group into groups to facilitate the implementation of training. (2) Assembly: General meetings of members of each group, public gatherings, and holding memorial weeks for the Prime Minister. (3) Schools: Establishing civil schools and special business supplementary schools. (4) Society: Establishing popular libraries, amateur clubs, various experimental fields, etc.

Section 4: Powers and Responsibilities of Party Departments and the Government towards People's Organizations (1) People's organizations are subject to the guidance of the Standing Department and the supervision of the government.

(2) When the Party department punishes the people's organization without guidance, it must submit it to the higher Party department for instructions, but the dissolution of the people's organization must also be transferred to the local government for execution in accordance with the law.

(3) When the government believes that the people's organization must be dissolved, it must handle it in accordance with the law, but it must notify the local Party department before execution.

University Presidents Praise Student Guide 175

The "Student Guide," published by the Diligence Bookstore at No. 198 Wangping Street, Sanma Road, Shanghai, was co-authored by 32 university presidents, professors, and experts, including Zheng Hongnian, Ouyuan Huai, Liu Zhanen, Liao Mao, Yu Jifan, Yu Fengbin, Jiang Wenyu, She Nanqiu, Li Quanshi, Tang Qingzeng, Pan Yangyao, Wu Yunrui, Jiang Xiangqing, Sun Benwen, Zhu Shaoping, Liu Linsheng, Wang Jin, and Zheng Xigu. It contains more than 200,000 words in two volumes. The first volume guides various students on their own status, the knowledge they should have, and the methods to prepare for advancement. The second volume details the methods of studying various subjects, the secrets of choosing a career to study abroad, etc. All are the results of the authors' research over the past 20 years and the opinions of experience. Mr. Cai Zimin praised the book as "Loving students with virtue and fulfilling the beauty of students." Recently, Luo Jialun, the president of Tsinghua University, Zhang Boling, the president of Nankai University, and Li Pei'en, the president of Zhijiang University, have all sent letters of praise, saying that the book is extremely helpful to students and should be in the hands of everyone. It is reported that the original price of each book is two yuan, but now, in order to popularize it, it is only sold for one yuan and two jiao, plus one yuan for postage by mail. The World Bookstore on Sima Road in Shanghai, the Dadong Bookstore, the Wenming Bookstore on Nanjing Road, the World Bookstore in Hangzhou, and bookstores in major ports all sell it on consignment.
